Senior Northern Route Generals Gu Zhutong and Others Take Office; Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Presents the Seal and Instructs Them to Complete the Bandit Suppression Mission; He Jian Delivers a Speech Stating That Bandit Suppression is the Central Issue of the Era 89

Nanchang Correspondence: Gu Zhutong, the Commander-in-Chief of the Northern Route of the Five-Province Bandit Suppression Army, and Jiang Dingwen, the Commander of the Northern Route Forward, after receiving their appointments, first took office and departed for the Nancheng-Nanfeng area to supervise the suppression. They returned to the province a few days ago and held a supplementary oath-taking ceremony today (23rd). Zhao Qilu, the Chief of Staff of the Northern Route Army Headquarters, and Liu Xing, the Commander of the Northern Route Forward, also took office at the same time. On that day, personnel from various military and political organs first held an expanded memorial week in the auditorium of the Provincial Government. Then, Xiong Shihui announced that they would wait for Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to attend. Chiang was inspecting in Nancheng Chongren and returned to the province via Fuzhou, arriving at 10:30 AM. After Chiang attended, he led the ceremony as usual and then personally presented the seal of the Commander-in-Chief of the Northern Route, which was issued by the National Government, to Gu Zhutong, and the seal of the Commander of the Northern Route Forward to Jiang Dingwen. Next, Gu, Jiang, Liu, and Zhao took the oath in order. After the oath, Chiang delivered instructions, saying, "The bandit suppression work in Jiangxi is now the key to the survival of the Chinese nation. Commander Gu, Commander Jiang, Commander Liu, and Chief of Staff Zhao, when the people of Jiangxi Province are in dire straits and the entire nation is in a critical state of survival, you are taking on the important task of suppressing bandits. This grand ceremony is of great significance because Jiangxi is the center of bandit suppression, especially the Northern Route. If the military operations for bandit suppression in Jiangxi can be successful, the other provinces will not be a problem. I hope that after Gu, Jiang, Liu, and Zhao take office, they will rectify the troops and work hard to suppress the bandits so that the evil bandits can be thoroughly eliminated in the shortest possible time, the bandit suppression mission can be completed, and the Chinese nation can be revived." Then, He Jian delivered a speech on behalf of the guests, saying, "Bandit suppression is the central issue of the era. The central issue of the first year of the Republic of China was the overthrow of the Qing Dynasty. The central issue of the fifteenth year of the Republic of China was the Northern Expedition. The central issue now is bandit suppression. Being able to solve the central issue of an era can complete the mission of an era. Being able to solve the central issue of an era can solve all the difficulties of the country and all the pain of society. Bandit suppression is the key to national revival. Bandits are a disease in the heart of the country. Without bandit suppression, we cannot resist Japan. Without bandit suppression, we cannot build. Without bandit suppression, we cannot revive the countryside. Without bandit suppression, we cannot unite internally. If bandit suppression succeeds, the nation will have a way out. If bandit suppression succeeds, it will be the first step towards national revival. Now the main force of the bandits is concentrated in eastern Jiangxi. The Northern Route Army has the important mission of annihilating the main force of the bandits. Today, Commander Gu, Commander Jiang, Commander Liu, and Chief of Staff Zhao took office, which is of great significance because the Northern Route is the focus of bandit suppression, and bandit suppression is the central issue of the era and the key to the era. I would like to represent all the officers and soldiers of the Western Route Army to wish Commander Gu, Commander Jiang, and Commander Liu victory in bandit suppression, and I am willing to work with them under the leadership of Chairman Chiang to complete the bandit suppression mission." Gu Zhutong then gave a response, saying, "The red bandits took advantage of the natural disasters and foreign insults that came one after another to spread poison and wreak havoc. The people in the border areas of Jiangxi, Guangdong, Fujian, Hunan, and Hubei cannot survive and cannot die. They obstruct national construction, restrain the central government from resisting insults, and hinder the progress of society, plunging the entire nation into eternal destruction. Therefore, the Central Government has determined that bandit suppression is the most important task at present and is devoting the nation's efforts to it. From now on, I will work with friendly forces under the guidance of Chairman Chiang to work hard to eliminate the evil red bandits and live up to the expectations of the officers and the people." The meeting adjourned at 11:30 AM with music. Gu Zhutong hosted a banquet today (23rd) to connect with the leaders of the senior military, political, and party circles in the province. It is reported that the Northern Route Headquarters has no less than 200,000 people under its command and is full of elites. After the general attack, the southeastern bandit areas of Jiangxi should be recovered in a few days. (October 23)

Inner Mongolian Prince De Wang Expresses Desire for Self-Preservation | Huang and Zhao Scheduled to Go to Guihua First | 90

Beiping Dispatch: The protagonist of the Inner Mongolian autonomy movement is Demchugdongrub, Vice-Chief of the Xilingol League. He is young and ambitious. After loudly advocating for autonomy, he often speaks of Genghis Khan's achievements, with a strong intention to follow in his ancestor's footsteps. He went to Japan in his youth and visited Ping once this spring, then went to Hankou to meet with Chiang Kai-shek, and met with key figures in Nanjing's central government. He currently has only over a thousand guns and less than two thousand soldiers, with very limited strength and shallow prestige. The various princes of Inner Mongolia hold a wait-and-see attitude toward the autonomy he advocates. Therefore, he has convened several meetings, but few attended. According to someone who personally attended the Bailingmiao meeting, the meeting convened in Bailingmiao starting on the ninth of this month was instigated by Prince De Wang alone. A total of 65 representatives from various leagues and banners attended, including two who traveled from Rehe. These two were Mongols from a puppet organization and are worthy of attention. One of them is a high-ranking military officer, which is particularly important. At the meeting, they vigorously advocated for autonomy, giving the meeting a political dimension. However, the representatives of various leagues and banners mostly adopted a wait-and-see attitude and suggested contacting the central government representatives before making a decision. Therefore, all proposals were reserved and postponed for discussion. As for the telegrams sent to the central government requesting autonomy, they were all drafted and sent by Prince De Wang outside the meeting and did not represent the consensus of the majority. Before the opening of the Bailingmiao meeting, Suiyuan Chairman Fu Zuoyi sent representatives to dissuade the princes of various leagues and banners in Suiyuan from attending, saying that the meeting had revolutionary overtones. The princes of various leagues and banners in Suiyuan did not think so and ultimately sent representatives. Therefore, from all aspects, the Bailingmiao meeting was a re-establishment of relations among the long-divided leagues and banners of Inner Mongolia and a non-political form of unity. It cannot change the general trend of the Mongolian people due to Prince De Wang's separate affiliation. Prince De Wang once told Ge Jun that Outer Mongolia has now been annexed by Soviet Russia, and Eastern Mongolia has been transformed into the territory of "Manchukuo." The Mongols, seeing the danger of the situation, are urgently seeking self-preservation. The current demand is only for self-preservation and autonomy, and there is no unreasonable request. Diplomacy is still handled by the central government, while other internal issues are handled by Mongolian autonomy. If the central government can allow this request, there will be no objection. If not, the Mongols can easily find another way out. However, the Mongols have no intention of fighting with the government. If, unfortunately, there is an accident, the initiators will not be the Mongols. According to Prince De Wang's statement, he does not intend to absolutely betray the central government, let alone other princes. The central government initially only instructed Chahar Chairman Song Zheyuan to handle the matter nearby. Song sent Xiao Zhenying to mediate. Later, considering the seriousness of the matter, the central government decided to send Huang Shaohong and Zhao Pilian to offer comfort. Huang and Zhao have arrived in Beiping one after another and decided to depart on the 26th, first to Suiyuan to meet with Suiyuan Chairman Fu Zuoyi, and then to Bailingmiao from Suiyuan. Fu Zuoyi sent a telegram to Beiping today to welcome them. The Ping-Sui Railway also prepared two chartered cars for Huang and Zhao, scheduled to depart from Xizhimen at 11:50 AM on the 26th. The Living Buddha Zhangjia will not travel with Huang and others. He plans to wait for reports from Li Shoushan and Gong Shishi, who were sent to Inner Mongolia for inspection, to arrive in Beiping and understand the real situation before proceeding. Yesterday, Mr. Huang spoke with He Yingqin and Huang Fu about everything and exchanged views with Zhangjia. This morning (24th), Mongolian princes in Beiping and representatives of fellow villagers in Beiping, including Prince Namjilebaoleng of the Jerim League, Prince Alatanwazir of the Khorchin Wing Banner, Song Yongweilu of the Jeridalhan Prince Banner, Wu Bao, Acting Jasak of the Khorchin Left Front Banner of the Zhe Banner, and Amurqingletu, representative of the Jerim League Chief, and Jierge Lang, Deputy Director of the Inner Mongolia Relief Committee, visited Huang. Huang was busy, so Zhao Pilian and Li Songfeng received them separately. Huang also plans to invite various Mongolian princes and important figures in Beiping tomorrow (25th) to solicit their opinions. According to Huang, the central government has already determined the principles for Mongolian affairs and will proceed according to the central government's intentions. Huang will first go to Guihua to meet with Chairman Fu before deciding on his next steps. He plans to inspect various leagues and banners and invite the princes of various leagues and banners to meet and convey the central government's intentions, planning to stay for several weeks. (October 24th)

Han Fuqu Returns to Jinan | Impressed with the North China Conference | Feng Yuxiang's Future Also Discussed 91

Jinan Dispatch: Shandong Provincial Government Chairman Han Fuqu went to Beiping from Jinan on the 16th of this month to attend the Beiping Political Reorganization Committee, to discuss North China's diplomatic, military, and political issues, and to report to He Yingqin and Huang Fu on the military and political situation in Shandong Province, and to discuss Feng Yuxiang's future and expenses. It was originally scheduled to return to Shandong around the 20th after the meeting closed. However, because he was very busy socializing in Beiping, he did not take a special train from Beiping to Nankou until late last night (22nd), and arrived in Jinan at 2:35 PM today (23rd). Those who returned with Han included Zhang Liansheng, Han Qinglin, Cheng Xixian, Chai Chunlin, and staff members. According to Han's statement, the gist was: "The North China Political Reorganization Committee meeting discussed the aftermath of the military and financial issues in North China. After Fang Zhenwu and Ji Hongchang left the army, the military issues have come to an end for the time being. As for the aftermath, although the conference discussed it in detail, there is no definite solution. The financial difficulties are quite difficult to solve, and the military expenses are particularly tight. Most of the soldiers receive seven or eight discounts on ten months' salary per year, or have only received five months' salary by now. There is no solution for next month's military expenses, and I feel that there is not enough military spending all day long. There are rumors in Beiping that North China's finances have a total deficit of more than 18 million, but the exact figure is not yet known. However, at this meeting, everyone was sincere and the impression was quite good. North China's diplomacy, since Chairman Huang returned to Beiping, has had a considerable solution and is absolutely not a problem, unlike the difficulties in the past. Sun Dianying went to Qinghai to reclaim land, but was blocked by Ma Hongkui when passing through Ningxia. Both parties sent telegrams to Beiping, but the Military Affairs Commission has no solution for this. Sun Dianying asked the Military Affairs Commission to issue an order that the unit not be dispatched for the time being, but the Military Affairs Commission has not made a clear statement. It is heard that Sun Dianying is sending people to contact various parties and is brewing something. Regarding Mr. Feng (Yuxiang)'s future and expenses, a considerable solution has been discussed and it is planned to apply to the central government to grant him the title of Director of Afforestation and Reclamation. It can be implemented after Feng agrees. Feng's monthly expenses require tens of thousands of yuan, and it is really difficult for Shandong Province alone to provide it. Feng is a member of the National Government and a member of the Central Committee, and his expenses should be allocated by the central government. Feng lives very comfortably and has not heard of any intention to leave. Shandong only provides a small amount of thousands of yuan as relief when it is absolutely necessary. Because of the financial difficulties in the province, I requested the Military Affairs Commission to reduce the province's army during the meeting in Beiping, but the Military Affairs Commission has not made any statement on this issue. As for how to handle it, nothing has been heard yet. Although the province's finances are quite difficult, because it is directly under the central government, it was not mentioned in the Political Reorganization Committee meeting. Although North China's military and politics are so difficult, the biggest key in China is still how the suppression of the Communists in Jiangxi progresses. If the suppression of the Communists has a solution, then all major events in the country will have a solution. If the suppression of the Communists in Jiangxi cannot be completed in one day, domestic rectification cannot be started in one day. Therefore, the most important issue at present is still the suppression of the Communists in Jiangxi. I went to Beiping from Jinan on the 16th, and the round trip took a total of eight days. In addition to attending meetings, I was receiving guests and had no free time. After a short rest in Jinan, I will go to Linyi, southern Shandong, at the end of the month to inspect county administration." (23rd)

Page 9

Eight-Province Food Conference Concludes | Chairman Chiang Attends and Gives Instructions | Resolutions on Various Rural Relief Cases 92

Nanchang Dispatch: The Eight-Province Food Conference held two group review meetings on the morning of the 23rd, and a general meeting in the afternoon to pass various proposals. It ended at 5:30 PM. Chairman Chiang was requested to give instructions by telephone. Chiang then arrived at the meeting by car from his private residence, first inspected the Provincial Party Headquarters and the Provincial Government for a week, and then went to the meeting place to call the roll one by one. Then he delivered instructions, and the meeting was adjourned at 7 PM. Xiong Shi presided over a banquet for the representatives in the West Flower Hall of the Provincial Government on behalf of Chiang, and it dispersed at midnight. The important proposals passed on the 23rd are recorded as follows:

Methods to Improve Sales and Production 93

China is established by agriculture and is inherently self-sufficient in rice. However, in recent years, various coastal areas have relied on foreign grain, which is difficult to fill the gap. The central provinces have surplus production, and the excess is increasing daily, forming two disadvantages that harm each other. Various provinces and cities should uphold the spirit of mutual assistance and regulate rice to supplement the insufficient with the surplus, in order to achieve self-sufficiency. (A) The provinces that produce rice should adopt the following policies. The main purpose is to select one or two commercial ports with convenient transportation within the province (such as Wuhu in Anhui, Jiujiang in Jiangxi, Changsha in Hunan, Hankou in Hubei, Wuxi in Jiangsu, and Shanghai) to concentrate rice for transportation and sales to other ports. Son, accumulation methods: (1) Various provinces and cities should follow the old Changpingcang system, raise public funds, and establish provincial and municipal warehouses to stabilize market prices. (2) Promote cooperatives to carry out purchasing, transportation, storage, and mortgage businesses. (3) Promote the banking and financial industries to attach new-style warehouse and grain businesses, and businesses to set up new-style warehouses to facilitate the storage of rice. Warehouses can issue warehouse receipts, and all receipts can be used to borrow from financial institutions. (4) Farmers' banks in various provinces should handle this business, and other banks and money houses should add agricultural product mortgages to provide funds for circulation. (5) Grain businesses, warehouse businesses, and stack businesses should jointly establish new-style rice mills to facilitate sales. (6) All grain businesses should establish close contact with the producing areas (referring to the nearby inland counties) to attract rice to the port for storage. Ugly, transportation methods: (1) Establish close cooperation with the transportation authorities in the selling area (referring to the coastal ports), and negotiate joint transportation and price reduction methods. (2) Establish close contact with the boatmen and shipping merchants in the producing area (referring to the nearby inland rice-producing counties), and negotiate contract transportation and unloading methods. (3) Various banks and money houses should add remittance mortgages to facilitate circulation. Yin, sales methods: The types, packaging, and weights of rice should be improved according to the wishes of the grain businesses in the selling area. (2) Grain businesses should establish close contact with grain businesses in the selling area and exchange market prices. Each grain business should send staff to reside in the selling area to attract customers to transport rice. (4) Encourage grain merchants in the selling area to open grain businesses here or send temporary brokers to handle rice. (5) Contact various military supply offices at any time to contract military food. (B) The provinces lacking rice should adopt the following policies. The main purpose is to purchase and transport rice from various domestic producing areas in succession according to the amount of rice lacking to meet the needs of the people. To the extent possible, the purpose is to persuade merchants not to purchase foreign rice. If it is unavoidable, the provincial and municipal governments must approve it if merchants want to purchase foreign rice before issuing a permit to show the restriction. (1) Estimate the types and quantities of rice lacking throughout the year and each month. (2) Investigate the harvests and storage amounts in various producing areas. (3) Tentatively purchase the types and quantities of rice from various producing areas. (4) Guide grain merchants to establish grain businesses or send brokers in the main domestic rice-producing areas to facilitate purchasing. (3) Establish close contact with grain businesses in various producing areas and report market prices to each other. The above are storage, transportation, and sales methods. The central government system is closely connected with the local area. Especially, internal and external cooperation should be carried out to achieve the greatest benefit of promotion. (1) Participate in the central control mechanism. The National Economic Commission has already decided to establish a grain control committee. It is proposed to add one member from each province and city to all the committee positions to participate and communicate opinions. (2) Raise funds for provincial and municipal warehouses. The current US cotton and wheat loans have been designated for the construction of the vehicle industry. It seems that a part of the loans should be designated specifically for provincial and municipal warehouse funds, to build warehouses and purchase surplus grain for regulating grain.

Restore All Levels of Granaries 94

Outline of the measures for restoring granaries: (A) System: (1) Central reserve granary, (2) Provincial reserve granary, (3) County granary, (4) Township granary, (B) Establishment: (1) The central reserve granary is established by the central government, and the provincial reserve granary is established by each province, both for storage and regulating grain prices. It is recommended that the central government and the provinces be instructed to plan and handle the granaries below the province. Township granaries must be established universally. County granaries should also be established separately according to local conditions. District granaries are inconvenient to set up at the same time due to local financial relations. Before township granaries can be established universally, it is proposed to postpone them temporarily. (City granaries are the same as county granaries, and town granaries are the same as township granaries) (2) The original old-system grain warehouses in various places should be restored immediately, and reorganized into county or township granaries according to the situation. (3) County or township granaries should combine the old Yishe granary system. County granaries should add reserve grain, and if there is still capacity, they can also manage agricultural granary businesses. (C) Organization: (1) The county granary organizes the County Granary Management Committee to manage all the county granary's activities. The managers are nominated by local professional groups, charitable groups, financial committees, and those who donate more than 100 yuan. The county magistrate is in a supervisory position and can investigate and audit at any time. (2) The reserve quantity of the county granary should be at least 2,000 shi of brown rice or 5,000 shi of grain, for fair price relief or loaning to township granaries. (3) The township granary organizes the Township Granary Management Committee, which is composed of several directors elected by the township who are wealthy and have a good reputation, and are jointly responsible for supervision. One director is rotated to be the director of the year, who is responsible for safekeeping. (4) The grain stored in the township granary must be at least 500 shi, for lending to poor farmers and fair price distribution. (D) Funding: In addition to the two methods of collection and donation prescribed by the ministry, it is proposed to collect the funding for county and township granaries by the following methods: (1) Old granary assets, (2) Public country deposits, (3) Accumulated local expenses that are not urgent, (4) County administrative fines, (5) Public property double price, (6) Incense association shrine public collection of funds, (7) Cooperative public funds, (8) Public funding, (9) Various subsidies. In addition to the above opinions, each province should refer to the Ministry of Interior's local granary management regulations and implement them conscientiously.

Chairman Chiang gave the closing speech, saying, "This food conference, inviting everyone to come here for a meeting, can be said to be the first major meeting related to the national economy and the people's livelihood. The food issue has never been studied in this way, especially the food issues related to several provinces, and there has not been a practical solution. That's why we invited the provinces to send you here to discuss a specific method of handling food. China is a country established by agriculture, and the country is filled with foreign goods, especially foreign rice. Food occupies an important position in the clothing, food, housing, and transportation mentioned by the Prime Minister. If the food issue is not resolved, all other issues cannot be resolved. The importance of the food issue is now being studied and paid attention to by countries around the world. The current world economy cannot be adjusted and merged. The second world war will soon be triggered. This is all because the food issue has not been resolved. China's food is oppressed by foreign food dumping. More than 10 years ago, it exceeded 440 million. The Prime Minister has made it clear in the Three Principles of the People and Nationalism. As for the next 10 years, it is especially unimaginable. It is becoming more and more critical. If we do not seek a solution urgently, I am afraid China will perish immediately. Since the September 18th Incident, the dangerous situation has become even more obvious. If this issue is not resolved one day, the national economy and the people's livelihood will lose their center of gravity one day, and all political and economic matters will not be able to be implemented. You are not only knowledgeable, but also familiar with the local conditions of the provinces and have rich experience. Before the Central Food Conference is convened, this conference is like a preparatory meeting, and the results of the conference will be contributed to the central government in the future, so that there will be a prototype first, and it can be seen in the management. Because I am inspecting the front, I just came back today and did not have time to participate in the meeting. I am very sorry, but I know the results of the meeting very well. Although the resolutions are simple, they are very practical. After the meeting today, we can follow the guidelines and take each case to solve the big problems of the national economy and the people's livelihood. But the meeting has been decided, and you always have to make an effect and a result, and really follow the decided guidelines to achieve the goal. We must work hard to manage ourselves, so that we will not fail this meeting and not fail your long journey. But Chinese people have always had a bad habit, which I would like to ask you to pay attention to, that is, many meetings often become empty words after the meeting, without any results, which is equivalent to not having a meeting, and only wasting money. But this food conference is not like other conferences. Food is a matter of life and death for the national economy and the people's livelihood. No problem is more important than the national economy and the people's livelihood. Don't say that food is only a part of the people's livelihood, and has nothing to do with the national economy. You must know that all national defense and self-defense national designs must be based on the food issue. For example, if we go to war with a foreign country, even if there is no military conflict, if the foreign country imposes an economic blockade on us and the country cannot be self-sufficient in food, everyone will have nothing to eat, wouldn't we starve to death, how can we talk about resistance and self-defense? Because it is so important, we called you here for the meeting. After the meeting, we will implement them one by one. Implementation is not easy, nor is it difficult, but in the effort of implementation, if everyone can understand that the food issue is related to the country, the people, and the survival of our own lives, then of course we will work hard to implement it. Everyone should be a model, and everything can be solved. What I am afraid of is sitting and talking but not taking action, then China can only be oppressed by foreign countries forever and cannot become strong. You must understand this point of reason. After you go back, you must tell your comrades the relationship between the national economy, the people's livelihood, and your own life, and implement it according to the resolution. What has been solved at today's meeting is not the word food, but the big issue of saving the country and the people. If the food issue cannot be resolved, then the work of saving the country and the people that we usually talk about is all fake. If we don't solve the food issue, we can't talk about other issues. May everyone have a share of strength and take a share of responsibility. These words are what I sincerely contribute to everyone, and I hope that everyone will work hard to complete and realize them." (23rd)

Jiangsu Provincial Government's Rural Relief Plan | Organizing Rural Financial Relief Committee | 95

The rural situation in Jiangsu Province has been extremely weak in recent years. Regarding the rural relief plan, the provincial government plans to organize a Financial Relief Committee, invite talents from all walks of life to design together, and specifically put forward the proposal passed at yesterday's meeting. It is reported that the important work of the committee is to first establish agricultural warehouses to regulate rural finance, or the provincial government purchases food, or the bank handles food storage and mortgage, and then stipulates the method according to the different situations of each county. The provincial government vigorously plans the warehouse buildings and local security conditions in each county to ensure safety. At a time when grain prices are extremely low and the rural economy is on the verge of bankruptcy, the warehouse issue is the most important plan. However, the autumn harvest is about to begin, and warehouses cannot be delayed, so it is planned to establish the committee as soon as possible in order to proceed in the shortest possible time. The temporary organization outline of the committee is recorded as follows: (1) The Jiangsu Provincial Government will establish the Jiangsu Provincial Rural Financial Relief Committee to regulate rural finance and improve the rural economy. (2) The tasks of the Rural Financial Relief Committee are as follows: A. Matters concerning the planning of agricultural warehouses and other adjustments to rural finance throughout the province. B. Matters concerning other suggestions for improving the rural economy and living conditions. C. The Rural Financial Relief Committee will have several members. In addition to the chairman of the provincial government and the heads of the Finance and Construction Departments as ex-officio members, the provincial government may designate or hire other relevant personnel to organize it together. D. This outline will be implemented from the date of promulgation. (25th)

Achievements of Road Construction in Anhui Province | 1,700+ Li Completed | 490+ Li to Be Completed 96

Anqing Dispatch: Liu Yiyan, Director of the Construction Department of Anhui Province, also serves as the Director of the Highway Bureau. During his term of office, he actively built highways. A total of 1,758 kilometers have been completed and opened to traffic, and approximately 490 kilometers will be completed soon. The recent status of each highway is recorded as follows:

National Highway 97

National trunk roads are being built in order according to the resolutions of the Seven-Province Highway Conference. (1) Beijing-Shaanxi Trunk Line: Enters the province from Jiangpu, Jiangsu, passes through Wujiang, He County, Hanshan, Chaoxian, Dianbu, Hefei, Liu'an, and Yejiaji to reach the border of Henan, with a length of 306 kilometers. The Wujiang-He, He-Chao, Chao-He, and He-Liu sections have been completed one after another to facilitate bridge-soil road traffic, and formal bridges and culverts are designed and reconstructed in stages. The roadbed of the 56-kilometer Liuye section has been completed, and bridges are being built. (2) Beijing-Sichuan Trunk Line: The same route as the Beijing-Shaanxi Line to Hefei, passing through Shucheng, Tongcheng, Gaohebu, Qianshan, Taihu, and Susong to reach the border of Hubei, with a length of 294 kilometers. The He-Gao and Gao-Tai sections have been opened to traffic long ago. The formal bridges and culverts rebuilt on the He-Gao section have been largely completed and will soon be fully completed. The construction of stone pavement on a sectional basis has been recruited by merchants. Formal bridges and culverts on the Gao-Tai section are also being designed. The remaining 54-kilometer Tai-Su section has been surveyed and prepared for construction. (3) Gui-Qi Trunk Line: Enters from Shangqiu, Henan, passes through Boxian, Taihe, Fuyang, Zhengyangguan, Liu'an, Shucheng, Tongcheng, Gaohebu, Anqing, Dongliu, and Zhizhi (formerly known as Qiupu) to reach Qimen, with a length of 562 kilometers. Except that the Shu-Gao section is the same route as the Beijing-Sichuan Trunk Line, the Bao-Zheng and Zheng-Liu sections have been completed and opened to traffic. Formal bridges are being built. The An-Gao section has been open to traffic for many years, and its bridges and crushed stone pavement have been completed long ago. The Construction Department has instructed the counties to build the Liu-Shu section, and the Liu-Huo and Shu-Huo branch lines can be used to open to traffic. The 180-kilometer section from Anqing to Qimen will be postponed due to limited funding. (4) Beijing-Guizhou Trunk Line: Enters from Jiangning, Jiangsu, passes through Dangtu, Wuhu, Xuancheng, Sunjiabu, Ningguo, Jixi, Shexian, Tunxi, Xiuning, and Qimen to reach the border of Jiangxi, with a length of 414 kilometers. The Jing-Wu section was opened to traffic a few months ago, and formal bridges, culverts, and stone pavement have been completed. The Wu-Xuan section, because the original road was the old base of the Ning-Xiang Railway, has been taken back by the Ministry of Railways and handed over to the Jiangnan Railway Company to rebuild the Wu-Zha Railway. Staff have been sent to survey the new line, and a team will be organized to set off to prepare for construction soon. The She-Tun and Tun-Xiu sections have been opened to traffic long ago and will be improved according to the Seven-Province Highway Engineering Standards. However, the Xuan-She section has been under construction for many years due to overlapping mountains, and it will be completed by the end of this year. The remaining section from Qimen to the border of Jiangxi has also been surveyed by the Construction Department together with the Jiangxi Committee.

Provincial Roads 98

Of the branch lines of provincial roads that connect the Jinpu Railway to the Huaihe and Guiqi main lines, there are the four roads of Mengfu, Mengbo, Mengbeng, and Mengsu, totaling 358 kilometers in length. All have been open to traffic for years. Those that connect the counties in western Anhui are the four roads of Liu-Huo, Huoshu, Tao-San, and Shan-Mao, totaling 166 kilometers in length. All have been open to traffic. Connecting Bengbu to Wuhu in the province is the Hebeng Road, which runs from Bengbu through Linhuaiguan and Dingyuan to Hefei, connecting with the Beijing-Shaanxi and Beijing-Sichuan main lines. It is 177 kilometers long and should be suitable for car traffic. Connecting Anhui and Zhejiang provinces are the Xuan-Chang Road, which runs from Xuancheng through Guangde to Changxing in Zhejiang Province, with 84 kilometers within Anhui. All formal bridges and culverts, as well as segmented road surfaces, have been completed. It is currently operated by a commercial automobile company. The Huihang Road, which runs from Tunxi through Yuling Pass to Hangzhou, has 60 kilometers within Anhui and can be completed within this month. The Tunchun Road, which runs from Tunxi to Chun'an in Zhejiang Province, has been surveyed by a team sent by the Construction Department. Although the project is costly, it is planned to be constructed. Connecting Anhui and Jiangsu provinces is the Jingjian Road, which runs from Wangniudun on the Anhui-Jiangsu border through Langxi to Shizipu, connecting with the Xuan-Chang Road. It is 36 kilometers long and will be open to traffic within the next month.

County Roads 99

Regarding county roads, those that have been completed and opened to traffic include the Ling-Gu, Wu-Si, and Chu-Lai roads. Those that are being surveyed and planned for construction include the Zhi-Dong, Chao-Wu, and Liu roads. Most of them are short in distance, and the projects are simple, making success easier. (October 22nd)

Recent News on the Songjiang Songxing Bankruptcy Case 100

In the bankruptcy case of Songjiang Bank, creditors Wu Boyang and others stated that after the bank's bankruptcy, the total amount of public and private deposits owed reached more than 600,000 yuan. After the creditors filed a lawsuit, the county court selected Xi Yushu and Xia Sunhuan to establish a liquidation office in early May of last year to begin liquidation. In July, a meeting of creditors was convened to report on the liquidation situation, including items described as secured loans without security documents and mortgaged loans without collateral, totaling more than 280,000 yuan. The office has successively filed lawsuits regarding the easily litigable portions and has already issued payments twice. All deposits above 200 yuan have been recovered by half. However, the creditors hope that the office can conclude within the statutory liquidation period and return the deposits, as they are accumulated from their hard-earned money. They have sent a letter to the office requesting a second report on the progress of the case, asking whether the 280,000 yuan without supporting documents is still under investigation.

A Net Boat Woman Hangs Herself and Dies 101

A woman named A'tang, daughter of Fei He, a net boat woman from the nineteenth district outside the South Gate, is in her teens. Her father died early, leaving behind a net boat. The mother and daughter fished along the shore to make a living. Recently, due to the scarcity of fish and shrimp, she was in dire straits and became resentful. On the night before last, she secretly went ashore while her daughter was unprepared, went to a collapsed house in the area, and hanged herself from a beam. The next morning, when A'tang saw that her mother was not there, she went ashore to look for her and discovered her, but she had already breathed her last.

A Peddler's Rush to the Festival Ends in Drowning 102

Recently, good-hearted locals in Lu Diao Wan Township raised funds to put on a play, attracting crowds of viewers from near and far, who came in groups, one after another. It was also reported that some people were setting up gambling dens there. As a result, ordinary peddlers saw it as a lucrative opportunity and rushed to the festival. Yesterday, three peddlers, Fan Yunsheng, Fan Jinxiang, and Shen Jinfu, who lived in Nanxinqiao in the city, hired a boat to go there with fruits. Unfortunately, while sailing through the NanJie Jing area on the dark night of the 24th, the boat accidentally capsized. Shen Jinxiang, who had some swimming skills, managed to stay afloat, but the Fan brothers both drowned. Fan Yunsheng was sixteen years old, and Fan Qingxiang was twenty-three years old. Their families were devastated to hear the news, as they depended on them for their livelihood.

A Suzhou Traveler Attempts Suicide by Poisoning at the Suzhou-Taiwan Hotel 103

A traveler arrived at Room 3 of the Xin-Suzhou-Taiwan Hotel outside the Lu Gate yesterday (the 24th) afternoon, claiming to be Wang Jinhou, 36 years old, from Shanghai, working as a merchant. At 9 p.m. that night, he asked the bellboy to bring stationery to write a letter and then went to sleep. Yesterday (the 25th) morning, the hotel discovered that the guest had taken poison and left a letter stating that he was doing this due to environmental pressure. He had eighteen yuan in cash and five jiao in small change to pay for the coffin. He also left a suitcase and a set of single shirts and pants as payment for the room and the bellboy's tips, etc. He was sent to Suyong Hospital, and his life is still in critical condition.

Four Families Robbed in Wuting Township 104

At 9 p.m. on the 23rd, a bandit boat suddenly arrived at Jinjia Village in Wuting Township, with more than a dozen bandits. They went to the homes of villagers Gu Jinchu, Gu Yangchu, Qian Fengsheng, and Qian Renzhai to rob them, resulting in a loss of approximately 500 yuan. The bandits fled towards Wusong Port.

Thugs in Suits Arrested for Robbery 105

Yao Yongquan, a sand dredger in Shifang Village, Huqiu, went to Qichang Gold Shop in the inner city of Changmen yesterday (the 25th) with his neighbor Mao Hongsheng to exchange gold ornaments, obtaining 65 yuan and 28 cents. They then went to a hotel on the road to drink. On their way home in the evening, they were suddenly attacked by two thugs in suits near Maojia Bridge, who grabbed them and took all their money. The security team chased after them and captured the thugs Zhu Zhongrun and Zhang A'gen, who were then handed over to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Former Finance Bureau Chief Embezzles Huge Sums 106

After Shen Bingchen, the former director of the Wuxian Finance Bureau, was transferred to the position of Jiangpu County Magistrate, the handover of affairs in Wuxian was not yet clear. It was discovered that Shen had embezzled public funds amounting to more than 60,000 yuan, including 10,000 yuan for defense expenses, 20,000 yuan for county expenses, 25,000 yuan for military expenses, and more than 4,000 yuan in other loans. The county government has submitted a request to the provincial government to demand repayment, and the provincial government has ordered Shen to settle the accounts clearly and hand over the public funds by a deadline. Furthermore, various institutions such as the Suzhou Land and Property Office were deeply surprised that Shen had embezzled more than 60,000 yuan during his tenure. Yesterday (the 25th), they sent telegrams to the provincial government, ordering him to hand over the funds.

A Large Group of Hubei Refugees Crosses the River in Jiangyin 107

Due to the impact of natural disasters and man-made calamities in Qichun County, Hubei Province, residents are unable to make a living. A large group of 136 refugees, men, women, old, and young, led by Chen Yijin, walked from Wuxi to Cheng, residing in the Tianhou Palace outside the North Gate. They also presented their permits from various counties to the Public Security Bureau for verification. On the 24th, they crossed the river to Jing.

Another Silk Merchant in Wuxi Disappears Due to Debt 108

Recently, the silk market has reached a state of extreme panic. Silk cocoon merchants in our county are all uneasy. Another six or seven silk factories have suspended operations. Recently, Xi Huian, the owner of Huisheng Factory, disappeared due to debt. Yesterday, Wang Xuchu, the owner of Hongren Silk Cocoon Company, also suddenly disappeared. Wang started as a silk broker, was skilled in maneuvering, and was accustomed to conducting speculative business. Every spring and autumn cocoon season, Wang would set up shops in the countryside to collect cocoons, often without cash, issuing cocoon tickets indiscriminately. As a result, the villagers suffered, while Wang became a wealthy man. In recent years, due to the severe drop in silk prices, he suffered considerable losses. This autumn cocoon season was particularly disastrous, leading to debts of more than 10,000 yuan. Feeling unable to cope, he also chose to run away. The creditors are now searching everywhere, hoping that Wang will return to Wuxi to settle the matter.

Pretending to Commit Suicide to Gain Sympathy and Defraud Money 109

Zhang Zhicheng, a native of Quzhou, Zhejiang, was formerly a partner in Zhang Rongchang Fruit Shop in this county. His wife, Du Guihua, was recently seduced and disappeared by Chen Zhaorong, a company commander of the Security Department stationed in Jiangyin. Unable to find her, Zhang went to Cheng to search but could not find her. He then untied his belt and hanged himself in a pine tomb in Feng Jing of the county's Hucheng District. He was rescued by villagers and sent to the Security Corps headquarters, where the deputy commander Zhao Zhongwen gave him travel expenses and contacted the Xicheng Long-Distance Bus Company to buy a half-price ticket for him to return to Xicheng and work in the shop. Unexpectedly, after Zhang came to Xicheng, he did not go to the shop but wandered around for several days. Having no money again, he re-enacted his suicide scene in a pine tomb in the low-lying fields near 319 Village in Hua Da Fang Zhuang of the 13th District. He was rescued by villager Yuan Peiliang, and Yuan Futang and others gave him ten silver dollars, advising him to return home. The incident was discovered by Wang Xuehan, a patrol officer of the First Substation of the Eighth Branch of the Public Security Bureau. Suspecting his motives, he interrogated Zhang, who was evasive. It was clear that he was pretending to commit suicide to gain sympathy and defraud money. He ordered the police to guard him and transferred him to the Eighth Branch. Yesterday (the 25th), he was transferred to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

An Old Man's Tragic Final Years Leads to Suicide by Drowning 110

On the 15th of this month, a male corpse was found floating in the Cao Wang Jing Bridge river in the 52nd Village of the 3rd District. He was old in age. The county court prosecutor, accompanied by officials, went to examine and confirmed that he had died by falling into the river. The village chief was ordered to provide a coffin and burial. It is now learned that the corpse was Qin Liangzu, an 86-year-old relative of the local gentry Qin Liangding, residing in Zhongshi Bridge Lane in the city. He suffered from mental illness and had a strange personality. In his youth, he had vowed not to marry unless he found a stunningly beautiful woman. So, at the age of sixty, he finally married Xiu Zhen, a daughter of an old man surnamed Huang from the South Gate. Xiu Zhen was twenty-nine years old. The following year, she gave birth to a son. Just as he was feeling fortunate, his beloved wife and son suddenly died one after another. Qin Liangzu's final years were tragic, leading him to develop a world-weary thought. One theory is that he accidentally fell into the river.

Yangzhou Water Police Rescue Four Hostages 111

Hangzhou Houchaomen Fire Kills an Elderly Woman 113

Xu Xinfa, a native of Shaoxing, moved from Shipailou to No. 8 and 10 Zhijie Street, Houchaomen, this spring and opened the Wanxiang Huichunlou Teahouse. At 3:30 a.m. on the 24th, he suddenly heard frequent sounds in the water tank in the backyard. He put on his clothes and went to look, seeing a fire in the tank with a fallen electric wire burning on the bamboo fence. He rushed to the nearby police station to report, and the police station relayed the report to the fire brigade and other fire-fighting organizations, which rushed to put out the fire. It took one and a half hours to extinguish the fire, which spread to No. 1 to No. 18 (No. 15, Faxi Temple, was not affected) and No. 6, 7, 8 of Liubuqiao, totaling 21 houses destroyed and 42 households affected, with losses of about 10,000 yuan. When the fire was raging, an elderly woman, Fu Xie, age 68, a native of Jiangxi, was unable to escape in her sleep and died in the fire. The scene was tragic.

Ningbo Zhenhai Ocean Surface Pirates Rob Coal Boat 114

The Siwei Coal Dross Company on the north bank of the Yongbu River previously purchased hundreds of tons of white coal from Shanghai. The other day, they hired the Jin Changfa sailboat to transport it to Ningbo. Unexpectedly, when the boat sailed to Zhenhai, near the ocean surface, it suddenly encountered a pirate boat, which ordered the coal boat to stop. More than twenty pirates swarmed over the boat. Seeing that the boat was only loaded with coal dross, they searched the boat, but without finding any silver dollars, they tied up a boat partner named Jia and left a calling card from the pirate leader, Xiang, instructing the other boat partners to inform the Siwei Company to prepare money and send someone to a certain mountain to redeem him. The boat arrived in Ningbo yesterday and reported the incident to the Siwei Company authorities, requesting them to investigate and find a way to rescue him.

This Port's Exports to the United States Increased Sharply in Nine Months; Almost Doubled Compared to the Same Period Last Year 125

According to the Continental News, Shanghai's exports to the United States in the first nine months of this year, according to statistics from the US Consulate General, almost doubled compared to the same period last year. Although this statistic only includes goods that require a price list to be filled out and reported, and does not include some goods subject to ad valorem tax in the United States, it can still provide a glimpse into the general state of exports to the United States. However, in the three months of July, August, and September, Shanghai's exports to the Philippines decreased significantly compared to the same period last year, while exports to Honolulu were roughly the same. Shanghai's exports to the United States in the first nine months of this year totaled US$7,317,341, while in the same period last year, they were only US$4,691,479. Shanghai's exports to the Philippines in the last three months totaled US$878,852, while in the same period last year, they totaled US$1,114,529. Shanghai's exports to Honolulu in the last three months totaled US$40,215, while in the same period last year, they totaled US$40,540. As for the prosperity of various goods exported to the United States, the situation often differs greatly from last year. For example, sesame seeds were only 43,860 pounds in the first nine months of last year, but reached 14,743,772 pounds this year. Tung oil was only 18,298 pounds last year, but reached 220,161 pounds this year. Tea leaves also increased from 2,207,395 pounds last year to 4,217,930 pounds this year. The total value of jade increased from 14,498 yuan to 286,410 yuan.

Fujian Gang Refuses to Load China Merchants Bureau Ships; To Transport Domestic Goods to Fujian for Cheap Sale; Believes it Impedes Their Business 127

The Shanghai National Goods Introduction Office transports goods to Fujian for cheap sale, which Fujian merchants believe hinders their business, causing great opposition from the Fujian Gang, involving the shipping company. The Fuzhou Gang refuses to load ships of the China Merchants Bureau because they transport goods from the National Goods Introduction Office to Fujian. The bureau collects freight from the Fujian Gang, which they also refuse to pay, drawing swords and bows, each going to extremes. The details are explored below:

Origin of Domestic Goods Entering Fujian 128

This year is the year of domestic goods. Leaders of various industries in Shanghai specially organized a National Goods Introduction Office to promote sales throughout the country at low prices. Fuzhou is also one of its distribution ports. Unexpectedly, the cheap sale of goods introduced by the National Goods Introduction Office to Fujian was welcomed by the people, but the commercial industry in Fujian suffered a major blow. If they lowered prices to compete, they would lose money. If they sold at the same price, no one would patronize them. All kinds of business were taken away by the National Goods Introduction Office. Therefore, the Fujian Gang strongly opposed the office. The Shanghai Sanshan Guild Hall is a gathering place for various commercial gangs in Fujian. For the sake of maintaining the business of each gang in the province, they negotiated to refuse the entry of goods from the National Goods Introduction Office into Fujian. Their method of obstruction was to negotiate with various commercial shipping companies to agree not to transport goods from the office. If they continue to load the goods, the Fujian Gang will stop loading goods with the shipping company.

Contacting Various Shipping Companies 129

Currently, there are four shipping lines operating on the Shanghai-Fujian route: Changan, Sanbei, Yihe, and China Merchants. The most frequent transport of goods from the Fuzhou Gang is handled by the customs declaration firms and passenger gangs affiliated with the Sanshan Guild Hall. Therefore, the Sanshan Guild Hall's cargo transport business is the largest. Since the incident of the National Goods Introduction Office, the Fujian Gang entrusted Wang of the Sanshan Guild Hall to contact various shipping companies, requesting them to consider Fujian's commercial industry and persuade the shipping lines not to transport goods from the office. If they continue to load the goods, the Fujian Gang will stop loading goods with that shipping company. As a result of the negotiations, Sanbei, Changan, and Yihe expressed their sympathy, and the Fujian Gang's struggle against the trend of domestic goods seemed to have come to an end.

China Merchants Loading Dispute 130

At that time, the shipping companies believed that the National Goods Introduction Office was only a temporary business, while the Sanshan Guild Hall was a fundamental transport business. Therefore, Changan first agreed, Yihe also agreed not to load, and Sanbei even held a banquet with the Fujian Gang in the guild hall. China Merchants Bureau initially permitted it, but recently the National Goods Introduction Office had several hundred pieces of textiles, etc., which were pledged to the bank, and loaded them onto China Merchants ships to enter Fuzhou. The Fujian Gang believed that China Merchants had violated its position and was still transporting domestic goods. Therefore, the Fuzhou Passenger Gang decided together to unanimously refuse to load China Merchants Bureau ships, refusing to load any import or export cargo from Shanghai and Fujian. The dispute arose from this.

Negotiations Between the Two Parties 131

The China Merchants Bureau believes that the transport of textiles to Fujian was arranged by the pledging bank, and the cargo owner had informed Wang of the Sanshan Guild Hall of the details in advance, fearing that it would cause a dispute. Moreover, the Bureau, with its state-run position, could not welcome this refusal in fact. After this refusal to load occurred, the China Merchants Bureau entrusted the Municipal Shipping Association to mediate. However, it was reported that the Fujian Gang must have a formal representation from the Bureau to prove that they would no longer transport their goods in the future before a settlement could be reached. This matter is feared to be difficult to accomplish, resulting in many Fujian gangs temporarily stopping the loading of cargo that had already been reported. The Bureau is now requiring the customs declaration firms to pay the freight for the goods that have already been recorded, but the Fujian Gang firmly refuses to pay. The two parties are insisting, and it is not known how to resolve it.

Taisun Sails to Fujian as Usual 132

The Shanghai Merchant Steam Navigation Bureau's Taisun, scheduled to sail to Fuzhou today, has suffered significant impact on its export cargo since the freight refusal incident. Many Hakka passengers temporarily stopped boarding. However, the Bureau has ordered the Taisun to proceed to Fujian on schedule, even if it sails empty, to maintain the route. Before the issue is resolved, freight between Shanghai and Fujian is mostly being transported by ships from Sanbei Yihong and other companies under the management of the Fuzhou Association. It is said that the Shanghai Merchant Steam Navigation Bureau is actively seeking methods for resolution.

According to a statement released yesterday by the Guidance Department of the International Trade Bureau, the value of goods imported into New Yiju Port from our country from April to June this year totaled 9,888,474 yuan. The main items included millet, tussah silk, and bean cakes, totaling 7,990,608 yuan, accounting for approximately four-fifths of the total. Coal, miscellaneous goods, soybeans, and raw salt were the next largest items, totaling 1,295,510 yuan, accounting for slightly less than one-eighth of the total. The remaining twenty items, such as lumber and fertilizer, accounted for less than one-fifteenth of the total, with a value of 600,256 yuan. The next largest items were Japanese socks, rubber boots, cotton yarn, cement, small mail packages, and fish, totaling 1,447,864 yuan. Finally, woolen fabrics and rice totaled 344,026 yuan. The total value of imports and exports was 16,810,453 yuan, with imports exceeding exports by 2,966,495 yuan.

The Ministry of Industry, recognizing that all alcohol used domestically relies on imports, has learned from customs investigations that alcohol imports in the Republic of China's 20th year (1931) totaled around five million gallons annually. Supplementary Measures After Ferry Service Inauguration: Drafted by Beijing-Shanghai, Tianjin-Pukou, and Beining Railways 135

Since the inauguration of the capital railway ferry, the results have been quite good. The Beijing-Shanghai, Tianjin-Pukou, and Beining Railways have now specially stipulated the following supplementary measures for the inauguration of the capital railway ferry: (1) The Shanghai-Beiping through train is designed for the convenience of through-transport passengers.

Seats on the Train 136

Should be allocated to through-transport passengers first. Any remaining seats may be allocated to passengers on the route as appropriate. The first- and second-class sleeping cars should primarily sell sleeper tickets. However, as the second-class cars are all sleeping cars, second-class passengers must purchase berth tickets. If berths are available, berth tickets may be waived, but only for through-transport and local passengers on the 301 down train and local passengers on the 302 up train. All second-class through-transport passengers on the up train must purchase berth tickets. (2) Shanghai-Beiping through train second-class berth tickets are priced at 2.50 yuan per night for the upper berth and 3 yuan for the lower berth. (3) Dining car seats may not be sold as passenger tickets. (4) Shanghai-Beiping through train tickets must be sold based on the number of sleeping berths and seats available in each class of car and must not be exceeded. (A detailed table of the number of sleeping berths and seats available on the Shanghai-Beiping through train and the schedule of rotations has been separately circulated to all relevant stations for notification and should be given special attention.) All relevant stations should coordinate the sale of sleeping berth and passenger tickets to avoid exceeding the number of berths and seats. For example, after the 302 train departs, if there are any remaining first- or second-class

Remaining Sleeping Berths 137

or seats, or third-class seats, the Shanghai North Station should telegraph the Suzhou Station. After the train departs from the Suzhou Station, if there are still remaining berths or seats, the Suzhou Station should telegraph the Wuxi Station. The remaining stops should follow this procedure accordingly. As for the 301 through train, when departing from the Nanjing Station, if there are any remaining first- or second-class sleeping berths or seats, or third-class seats, the Nanjing Station should telegraph the Zhenjiang Station. The remaining stops should follow this procedure accordingly. (5) Stations wishing to reserve first- or second-class sleeping berths on the 302 train should telegraph the Shanghai North Station information desk. Those wishing to reserve second-class sleeping berths on the 301 train should telegraph the Nanjing Station. (6) The freight charges for luggage and parcels transported on the Shanghai-Beiping through train should be calculated according to the through-transport mileage listed in the Shanghai-Beiping through train fare schedule. (This fare schedule is currently being compiled by the Through Transport Department of the Ministry of Railways and will be distributed to all relevant stations for application upon issuance. The original 50 kilometers between the Beijing and Pukou sections in the schedule have been removed.) The river crossing fee stipulates that luggage will be charged 5 cents per 20 kilograms. Less than 20 kilograms will also be calculated as 20 kilograms, with a minimum charge of 10 cents. Parcels will be charged 3 li per kilogram for the river crossing fee, with a minimum charge of 10 cents. (6) Above

Luggage and Parcels 138

River crossing fees and passenger fares have been stipulated, no other donations or fees may be added, nor may they be reduced due to various discount tickets. All those not crossing the river by ferry will continue to be handled in accordance with current procedures. (7) Shanghai-Beiping through train tickets and all tickets supplemented on the Shanghai-Beiping through train will be printed with the four red characters "Shanghai-Beiping Through Train" for clarity, and a red horizontal line will be added above the "Shanghai-Beiping Through Train" characters to indicate that it includes the extra fast train surcharge. Measures for Charging for Storage of Mutually Transported Materials Between Railways: Railway Ministry Instructs Railway Bureaus to Comply 140

Regarding the measures for charging for the storage of mutually transported materials between railways at stations, the Ministry of Railways yesterday specifically instructed the railway bureaus, saying that according to Article 32 of the General Rules for Freight Transport (If goods are stored at a station or railway freight yard, the railway may charge storage fees in accordance with the provisions and prices set by the railway.), this railway charges ordinary merchants storing goods at stations according to the grade of the goods. The railway charges storage fees for goods that the railway is responsible for, calculated at 3 jiao 5 fen per ton for first-class goods per 24 hours or less than 24 hours, 3 fen per 50 kilograms, 3 jiao per ton for second-class goods, 2 fen 5 li per 50 kilograms, 2 jiao 5 fen per ton for third-class goods, 2 fen per 50 kilograms, 2 jiao per ton for fourth-class goods, 1 fen 5 li per 50 kilograms, 1 jiao 5 fen per ton for fifth-class goods, 1 fen per 50 kilograms, and 1 jiao per ton for sixth-class goods, 5 li per 50 kilograms. If the goods are the responsibility of the owner, the storage fee is reduced by half according to the above price rates. If the goods are stored at this railway's material factory, regardless of grade, the charge is 4 jiao 5 fen per ton per month. However, the freight charges for mutually transported materials between railways are not graded. When materials from other railways are stored at this railway's stations, the charge is 4 jiao 5 fen per ton per month. When materials are stored at this railway's stations, should the storage fee be charged according to the grade of the materials, as with ordinary goods, or should a separate price rate for the storage of materials from other railways be set? Please review and instruct. After investigation, materials mutually transported between railways are generally escorted by this railway. The station storage fee should be reduced by half as for goods the owner is responsible for, to show mutual benefit. In addition to instructing and separately instructing, you are hereby ordered to comply. The bureau has forwarded this order to the traffic department for compliance.

Tragic Situation of Compatriots in Northeast Under Japanese Military Boots: Representative of Wang Delin's Troops Reports to Shanghai 141

Liu Yicheng, representative of Commander Zhang Yuting of the Northeast Volunteer Army General Commander Wang Delin's troops, came to Shanghai yesterday under orders from the Jilin front. He reported on the recent tyrannical and brutal behavior of the Japanese army in various parts of the Northeast, including the slaughter of the people. The facts are hereby announced to the people of the country and recorded as follows:

Arson, Destruction of Houses, Rape, and Murder 142

On September 22, Zhang Yuting, the Director of Military Operations of the Volunteer Army, departed from Dongning Nanquanzigou and led his troops to attack the Japanese army. On September 23, they arrived at Yantongyazi. Zhang's headquarters was located in the Xu family compound. Xu Jiashan, the steward of the compound, was the head of a hundred households in the area. Mr. Xu was humble, righteous, and particularly enthusiastic about saving the country. When Zhang's troops entered the area, Mr. Xu spared no effort to run around and raise supplies. The local people were also happy to help, bringing food and drinks to support the national salvation army. Later, on September 24, the Volunteer Army advanced to Twenty-Eight Daohazi and engaged in repeated fierce battles with the Japanese army, but retreated due to insufficient ammunition. After the retreat, the Japanese army first set fire to the civilian houses in Yantongyazi, then found the Xu family compound, accused Xu Jiashan of collaborating with the enemy, and bound him and hanged him. He was beaten with iron bars, leaving his body covered in injuries. He cried out and died. Many young women in the neighboring houses to the left and right of the compound were first violated and then stabbed to death. One child who cursed the Japanese for their barbarity was impaled with bayonets and used as a plaything, screaming in agony until death.

Arbitrary Arrests, Hand Chopping, and Foot Mutilation 143

At the same time, a dozen civilian houses in Twenty-Eight Daohazi were also destroyed and burned. People were captured everywhere and interrogated about whether they had any connection with the Volunteer Army. Those who did not confess were subjected to horrific torture. Some had their hands chopped off, others had their feet mutilated, and still others had only their ears and noses cut off or the tips of their tongues cut off, left neither alive nor dead, rolling on the ground screaming in agony. The sight of blood and flesh was everywhere, and anyone with a conscience could not help but grieve.

Airplanes Drop Bombs, Flesh and Blood Flying 144

Also, at the beginning of last month, when the Volunteer Army led by Wu Yicheng, Zhang Yuting, and Liu Shunqing attacked Dongning, the Japanese and puppet troops in the city were weak and about to collapse. Therefore, several aircraft were dispatched to bomb the city extensively. In addition to some casualties among our Volunteer Army, the residents inside and outside the city were also affected. The most tragic case was that of an old farmer's family. The family of four, including the husband, wife, and children, made a living by raising livestock and pulling carts. As the old farmer was feeding the livestock, an airplane flew over and dropped a heavy bomb, instantly killing the entire family, including the livestock. Flesh and blood flew everywhere, a sight too gruesome to bear. Commander Zhang, deeply saddened by the repeated and unwarranted injuries inflicted upon the people by the violent Japanese, has reportedly asked General Commanders Wang Delin and Kong Xianrong for instructions to provide compensation and aid the injured and comfort the people.

Jin Shuishan's Nationality Verified: Confirmed to Be Chinese 152

Fuxing Society reported that Jin Shuishan, a student at the Central Artillery School, requested leave to return to his hometown (Guangdong) during the summer vacation. He transferred to Shanghai from Beijing and took the Yisun steamer south. Unexpectedly, the Japanese Consulate General identified him as a Korean revolutionary and, together with the Municipal Public Security Bureau's water patrol team, arrested Jin when the Yisun weighed anchor, detaining him at the team and transferring him to the Municipal Public Security Bureau. Because Jin claimed to be from Guangdong, the Municipal Public Security Bureau refused extradition and sent Jin to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters. The Japanese Consulate General then requested extradition from the headquarters, but it was ultimately refused because Jin's nationality was unclear. It has been almost three months to this day. A Korean expatriate told the Fuxing Society reporter yesterday that after the Songhu Garrison Headquarters took Jin into custody, it sent letters to the Central Artillery School and the Guangzhou Municipal Public Security Bureau to inquire about Jin's nationality. The Central Artillery School replied that Jin's registration form listed his籍貫 as Guangdong. The Guangzhou Municipal Public Security Bureau also replied that the Jin surname and the names of his parents were recorded in the Guangzhou household register, proving that Jin was undoubtedly a Chinese citizen.

The origins of the China National Cotton Fabric Market Co., Ltd. The passenger transportation business of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway has always been comprised of about half tourists, and among the tourists, foreign visitors account for a considerable number. Various measures for protection, renovation, improvement, and promotion will be implemented separately, aiming to make guests feel at home and make travel convenient for tourists. The hope is to promote our country's inherent culture and change foreigners' misconceptions. Ministry of Communications Plans Postal and Telegraph Merger; Third and Fourth Class Telegraph Bureaus to be Merged into Post Offices; Implementation Expected by January Next Year; Additional Telegraph Lines to be Laid Between Beijing and Shanghai 158

A Central News Agency report states that Zhu Jia-hua, Minister of Communications, in order to facilitate telegraph delivery and save expenses, has decided to merge postal and telegraph services and to construct a Beijing-Shanghai telegraph line along the Beijing-Shanghai Highway within this year. A Central News Agency reporter inquired about this matter yesterday morning with Hua Jinghan, business manager of the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau, who stated the following:

Postal and Telegraph Merger 159

Regarding the postal and telegraph merger, the bureau has not yet received a formal order from the ministry. However, it is understood that the Ministry of Communications, in order to facilitate delivery and save expenses, has decided to implement this in the shortest possible time. Therefore, the Ministry of Communications specially sent Zhou Jiyao, head of the Sixth Division, to Shanghai a few days ago to discuss merger procedures with Peng Yuyi, the national line director. It is heard that the merger method has been decided, with all third and fourth class telegraph branches in various locations being merged into the local post offices. This should result in significant savings in terms of delivery and expenses. It is expected that this can be implemented by January next year.

Additional Lines Between Beijing and Shanghai 160

Because traffic between Beijing and Shanghai is becoming increasingly dense and the existing telegraph lines are insufficient, the Ministry of Communications has decided to construct a Beijing-Shanghai telegraph line along the Beijing-Shanghai Highway in the coming days. All materials have been transported and are currently being inventoried. Construction will begin shortly on four sections: Beijing-Zhenjiang, Zhenjiang-Wuxi, Wuxi-Suzhou, and Suzhou-Shanghai. It is scheduled to be completed by early December of this year and put into operation by the end of the year.

New Machines Arriving Soon 161

The Ministry of Communications, recognizing that the existing telegraph machines in various bureaus are outdated and slow, has ordered more than 30 of the latest telegraph receivers and transmitters from abroad. Two machines have already arrived in Shanghai and have been installed in the Beijing and Shanghai bureaus, respectively. As a result, telegraph delivery between Beijing and Shanghai is now faster than before. Six more machines are expected to arrive in Shanghai next month. Once all the new machines have been delivered and installed, communication throughout the country can be accelerated significantly, it is said.
