The Malayan Team Lost to the Western Team in Last Night's Water Polo Match | Five to Two | ▲ No Winner Decided in the Mixed Relay 226

The Malayan swimming team, organized by Guangdong and Hong Kong athletes, lost again to the Shanghai Western team by five to two in the third water polo match last night. The match was held at the Xiqing Swimming Pool at 7:30 PM. The audience was still crowded. Because the Western team was more familiar with the venue, had better physical fitness, and more accurate shots, they scored four goals in the first half. In the second half, the Malayan team fought bravely and scored one goal, but carelessly, the Western team scored again. In the end, the Malayan team scored a penalty goal. The final score was five to two, and the Western team won. Chen Qisong, a Malayan general, was absent due to illness and was replaced by Xu Heng, which also affected the team's strength. The list of both teams is as follows:

▲ Malayan Team: Xu Heng, Chen Fuxing, Wang Xinmin, Huang Jiliang, Guo Zhenheng, Shi Jinpei, Yang Henghua

▲ Western Team: Davis, Wastoff, Johnston, Faping, Sinclair, Baron, McLester

▲ Mixed Relay 227

Miss Yang Xiuqiong was absent, which was disappointing. The Malayan team then became three men and one woman: Chen Fuxing, Shi Jinpei, Xu Heng, and Miss Liang Yongxian. The Western team was Haite Lai, Miss Biling Si, Haimeng Te, and Miss Neil. As a result, both teams arrived at the same time, with no winner decided. The time was one minute and fifty-nine seconds. Chen Fuxing was behind Haite Lai in the 50-yard swim, but Shi Jinpei was far ahead of the opposing woman, Biling Si. In the final 50-yard swim, Liang Yongxian was ten yards ahead of Neil. Neil tried desperately to catch up, but they arrived at the same time, with no winner decided. Both sides were satisfied.

▲ Swimming with Bound Feet 228

Before the water polo match, there was also a performance by the Yang Henghua and Yang Yuanhua brothers, who performed swimming with their hands and feet bound. Both their hands and feet were tightly bound, and they were able to swim back and forth for a distance of 75 yards. They were truly men becoming fish.

The Shi Brothers Successfully Crossed the Yangtze River in Less Than Twenty-Three Minutes. Thousands of People Watched, Creating a Grand Scene. 229

(Reuters, Nanjing, 25th) The Shi brothers will attempt to conquer the rapids of the Yangtze River this afternoon, swimming from Pukou to Nanjing, a distance of about ten li or three miles.

▲ The Shi Family Has Four Talents This is an unprecedented feat in Chinese history. At this time of year, the weather is cold, and the river water is high, making it even more dangerous. The Shi family are all famous swimmers. The eldest brother, Shi Xinglong, is known as the "Water Monster" and has represented China at the Far Eastern Games. The second brother, Shi Xingzhi, broke the national record in the 400-meter freestyle with a time of 5 minutes and 51.5 seconds and the national record in the 1500-meter freestyle with a time of 23 minutes and 27.6 seconds at this year's National Games. Miss Shi Ruisheng won fourth place in the women's 200-meter freestyle. The Shi family has four talents: three brothers and one sister, from Dalian, representing Liaoning at the National Games. All four talents will participate in today's crossing of the river.

The Shi family crossing the river, from right to left: Xinglong, Ruisheng, Xingzhi, Xinglu.

▲ A Petition That Is Heartbreaking to Read 230

In the letter submitted to the Nanjing Municipal Government requesting permission for this feat, it is stated, "We are from Liaoning Province, and we want to make the people not forget the Northeast. Therefore, we secretly returned to Nanjing to participate in the National Games. Today, the grand event has come to an end. Athletes from all over the country are returning home with smiles of victory, but we can only look at the medals and weep. We have a home, but we cannot return home. We are abandoned in this vast sports field, like homeless swallows. The fate of the country is not good, and the nation is perishing. The small island of the Eastern Neighbor has seized our three provinces. In order to awaken the people's attention to recovering the lost territory, we have completely ignored the danger and coldness of the Yangtze River's waters. Therefore, we have decided to swim from the east bank of Pukou to Nanjing on October 25th."

▲ Approved by the Nanjing Municipal Government 231

The Nanjing Municipal Government has approved this request. To prevent accidents, it has contacted the Nanjing Police Department to make arrangements. Special police officers have been dispatched to both sides of the river to provide protection. The Navy has also dispatched a steamboat to provide protection. The eldest brother, Shi Yulong, gave his youngest sister a final warning not to participate in this feat, because although Miss Shi has a particularly strong physique and high swimming skills, her young age is a serious obstacle.

▲ The Grand Occasion of Crossing the River 232

(Nanjing, 25th Dispatch) The Northeastern youth swimmers Shi Xinglong, Xingzhi, and Xinglu successfully swam across the Yangtze River from Pukou on the afternoon of the 25th, arriving at the Xiaguan Ferry Terminal in 22 minutes and 27.2 seconds. Tens of thousands of Nanjing citizens watched, and more than ten thousand people stood along the riverbanks. The Shi brothers crossed the river at one o'clock and first went to the Jinpu Railway Bureau to ride the Lin Tong charter steamer with Qiu Wei, the committee chairman of the railway bureau, and representatives of the Nanjing Municipal Government to Xiaonan River, upstream of Pukou. They entered the water at 3:27 PM. Lin Tong reduced its speed and followed behind. The Ninghai Navy dispatched two speedboats, and the Capital Police Department dispatched three patrol boats. Three lifeboats from the water police patrolled to provide protection. Many spectators hired steamers or small boats to watch. At one time, the river was filled with masts and sails, creating a grand scene.

▲ Spectators Celebrate Success 233

The Shi brothers were fastest on the north bank. When they reached the middle of the river, the water was turbulent, and they stood upright in the water to rest briefly. Xingxie was in the lower reaches, leading the way. The youngest brother, Xinglu, was in the middle, and the eldest brother, Xinglong, was on the right, providing protection. They were less than two meters apart. Because the bank was steep and there were many people, they changed to landing at the ferry terminal at the same time. The spectators on the river and along the coast cheered and shouted slogans celebrating their success. The entire journey was more than 3,000 meters and took less than twenty-three minutes. If they had not been affected by the waves from the small boats, and Xinglong had not had to protect Xinglu, the results would have been even better.

▲ The Railway Bureau Presented Silver Cups 234

The Shi brothers went to the Ninghai warship to take a bath and rest. At about 5:00 PM, they took the charter steamer back to Pukou to attend a welcome party held by the Jinpu Railway Bureau. Qiu Wei and Yu Huang, the representative of the Special Party Department of the Jinpu Railway, delivered speeches. Guest Feng Zhaoji gave a speech. Then Xinglong gave a speech. The Railway Bureau presented silver cups and iron flags. They returned at 6:30 PM.

▲ A Brief History of the Shi Brothers 235

According to Mr. Zhu, a close friend of the Shi family, Xinglong graduated from a Japanese technical school and is now auditing courses at Central University. He has been swimming for six years and has won the swimming championship at the previous National Games and attended the Far Eastern Games. Xingzhi is 18 years old and is studying in the third grade of the First Middle School established by the Japanese in Dalian. He has been swimming for four years and won the 400-meter and 1500-meter championships at this year's National Games, breaking the records. Xinglu is 16 years old and is studying in the same grade as Xingzhi. He has only been swimming for three years. The youngest sister, Ruisheng, is 12 years old and has only been swimming for six months. She won fourth place in the 200-meter freestyle at this year's National Games, which can be called a genius. Ruisheng also wanted to participate in the crossing of the Yangtze River, but was dissuaded by her brother. Xingzhi, Xinglu, and Ruisheng are scheduled to leave Nanjing for Jinan and then Qingdao on the morning of the 27th and take a boat back to Dalian. Xinglong will stay in Nanjing.

Over a Thousand Spectators Unanimously Appreciate Xu Qiu's Performance, with No Winner Decided. High Pressure and Low Draw Each Have Their Own Housekeeping Skills. It Was Cold and Late, and We Parted Peacefully. 236

The Cycle of Mutual Generation and Restraint 237

The tennis skills of the three musketeers, Qiu, Lin, and Xu, each have their own strengths. Lin and Xu are equal in serving, but Qiu is too weak. The baseline long draw is Qiu's specialty, and both the left and right corners have power. Xu's left corner is slightly weaker. The net interception should be attributed to Lao Lin, and the high pressure ball is especially given to Xiao Xu. Sincerely, each has its own merits, and it all depends on the opportunity and the wonderful use of it to surpass victory. Therefore, the past battles of the three heroes have created a cyclical situation. The five elements restrain each other and can generate each other. Only three heroes are competing for hegemony, and I don't know who can win the title of national player.

Qiu Feihai Goes Smoothly All the Way 238

Yesterday, Xiao Xu was delayed and did not start the game until 3:15 PM. Lao Qiu first won two games with four two four one. When it was Xiao Xu's turn to serve in the third game, he was fierce and powerful, making Lao Qiu unable to resist four times in a row. After Lao Qiu passed this level, he used his low draw skills to repeatedly oppress Xiao Xu, who retreated to the baseline. Except for the fifth game, which was still won by Xu, he went smoothly all the way and won the first set with six to two.

Xu Chengji Uses a Little Skill 239

In the second game, Xiao Xu, in view of the terrible long draw oppression of Lao Qiu, repeatedly won with serving on the one hand, and used a little skill on the other hand, lightly hitting short balls very close to the net. Lao Qiu ran east and west and could not cope, and first won two games. Qiu then fought with all his strength, creating a two-to-two tie. Later, Xu won three more high ball opportunities and one serving all-out victory, and pulled back the second set with six to four.

The Third Set Was the Most Competitive 240

The third set was the most competitive between the two sides, and the performance was also the most exciting. Lao Qiu was full of energy and vigorously抽擊. Xiao Xu was patient and calm, avoiding his sharp edge, sometimes far and sometimes near, or left or right. At first, Qiu took the lead with two one three two. The sixth and seventh games were won by Xu, that is, with four three, five four, six five, and reversed the defeat to victory. Then he created a seven-to-seven tie. Finally, Xu won two more games in a row and won the third set with nine to seven.

The Fourth Set Ended Peacefully 241

The third set came to an end. Both sides rested for a while and re-entered the court. This game was a critical moment. If Xiao Xu won again, it could end. At first, Xu won a game every time he served, and had created a three-to-three tie. After the fourth game, Qiu won three games in a row and finally pulled back a game with six to three, creating a two-to-two tie. Qiu had the intention to continue the battle, but at this time it was already twilight and the evening breeze was blowing. Xiao Xu was unwilling to hurt the harmony again, so he ended the game without deciding a winner.

Common Sense

Qin People Have No Time to Grieve for Themselves 251

— Xianxian

The athletes from Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang provinces, who participated in the National Games held in the capital this time, when they marched in formation at the stadium, it is said that among the audience, amid "very enthusiastic" applause, many shed tears. Needless to say, in this joyful atmosphere, the reason for "shedding tears" was naturally for these athletes, who are already pitiful creatures "unable to return home." Indeed, when we read the declarations of the Northeast athletes and the speeches of Party and state figures, all with "recovering lost territories" as the backbone, even we who live in the blessed land where we have never heard the sound of cannons from the Northeast cannot help but "shed a tear of sympathy."

In this "Northeast War, coming to a temporary end," "remnants of Fang's troops, already suppressed," "lost counties, successively recovered," "Japanese goods imported into China, soaring," and "Sino-Japanese situation, showing promise" of a "gradually improving" period of tranquility, the National Games suddenly released such a "tear gas," I wonder if it can raise the public's "minute of fervor" again.

Whether "East Asian peace" can be as stable as Mount Tai under the establishment of "Manchukuo," even if "King Wen were reborn," I fear his "divine divination would be ineffective," because to maintain "East Asian peace," one must inevitably cover the entire Asian continent with the Rising Sun Flag. To achieve this, one must first eliminate the land threat from Soviet Russia and the maritime threat from the United States. Once these two major threats are eliminated, then close the door and devour the entire China alive. At that time, we young masters in this blessed land will probably be in the same position as the people of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang today, and there will be no audience to "shed a tear of sympathy" amid "very enthusiastic" applause.

The Qin people had no time to grieve for themselves, and later generations grieved for them. Later generations grieved for them but did not learn from them. Everyone, please close your eyes and think, what is the next sentence? The athletes from Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang provinces are already unable to return home, and we who live peacefully in this blessed land "shed tears" for them amid "very enthusiastic" applause. But we who live peacefully in this blessed land and "shed tears" for the Northeast athletes amid "very enthusiastic" applause, if "shedding tears" is all we do, everyone, please close your eyes and think, what will happen in the future?

The Secret of "Pulling" 252

— Jian Yin

Recently, there have been articles about "pushing" and "pulling" published in the newspapers. Examining their content, they are nothing more than teaching the secrets of "pushing" and "pulling" in how to conduct oneself in the world. In fact, the way to conduct oneself is not limited to "pushing" and "pulling" alone. According to my observations, there is also a "pulling out" (拔) principle. "Pushing" means pushing others into the fire pit, and "pulling" means pulling someone up and running, like a rickshaw driver, regardless of direction. But "pulling out" is different. When someone is unsteady on their feet and walking onto the Bridge of Helplessness (奈何橋), you pull the bridge away, and the person falls into a deep abyss. This is the function of "pulling out," which is naturally different from the others.

"Pulling out" also has two types: "frontal pulling out" and "reverse pulling out." "Frontal pulling out" means doing things openly and pulling someone's feet out in front of them. One pull and they fall. "Reverse pulling out" means taking advantage of someone's unpreparedness, like shooting a cold arrow, pulling their feet out from behind, causing them to fall backward. However, "frontal pulling out" is not as easy as "reverse pulling out."

It's fine if someone doesn't want to accomplish anything in society. But if you want to accomplish something, you must steadily establish your footing, otherwise you will inevitably "end in utter failure." Suppose you only care about appearances, even if you are outstanding and have great strength, do you think you can be unafraid of others? No! It is precisely because you have great strength that people won't compete with you directly. They will simply squat down and pull your feet out, and you will fall without a doubt. This is because you haven't established your footing! This is "frontal pulling out."

At the same time, even if you have established your footing, do you think you can be worry-free? Who knows, the person pulling you won't pull you to your face. Instead, they will hide behind you, insert their hands between your feet, and pull backward with all their might. You will still inevitably fall. This is the function of "reverse pulling out." Even if you are highly skilled, it will be in vain!

Those who know the power of "pulling out" don't want to give up so easily. Even if you pull them down, they can still climb onto the stage. Thinking that this way, they can avoid the danger of being pulled. Little do they know, the person who wants to pull you out will dismantle your stage. In other words, they won't pull your feet, they will pull out the stage you're standing on. "Pulling out the stage" is the same as "pulling out the feet." Eventually, you will fall again. Then the person who pulled you out can climb onto the stage themselves. But if you want revenge, you can pull their feet out in the same way, remember?

A Brief Record of Whale Watching 253

— Gao Yahun

Recently, there has been a sensation in this city about a large whale. Driven by curiosity, I also spent half a day's pay to go and see it. Haha! It's true that seeing is believing. This whale had probably been out of the water for a long time, so it had a stench. Its black skin was as smooth as if it had been oiled. Its entire body was not more than a hundred feet long, and its weight certainly did not exceed ten thousand pounds. It can be seen that the stories in Shanghai are often exaggerated. Compared to what I saw more than ten years ago in Zhenlongdian, Shaoxing, it was a world of difference. Now, I will introduce what I saw to those in this city who have seen the big whale:

A seagoing ship, loaded with salt bags, was leaving Zhenlongdian, heading for a certain port. When it reached the middle of the sea, it was already late, and in the haze, they saw a black mountain blocking their path. The captain of the ship was very careful and familiar with the harbor, so he was very surprised and suspicious. Upon closer inspection, he was extremely alarmed. Because this black mountain was slowly moving closer to the ship. This was not a sea monster, but certainly a fish monster. He immediately ordered to turn back the sails and try to return. Before a moment passed, although the ship was as fast as an arrow, the black mountain moved closer to the ship even faster. The people on the ship were all silent and worried, as they vigorously sailed. The black mountain moved closer and closer to the ship, and a mist-like drizzle splashed onto the stern. The captain knew that the situation was critical. He immediately took the salt bags from the hold and frantically threw them into the sea at the stern. Although the black mountain was still following, it sometimes rose and fell on the horizon. The captain knew that this was a sign of the big fish swallowing the salt bags. So, he kept throwing salt bags. As the ship's load lightened, it moved faster. As the sky was about to dawn, they returned to the original port. The tide had also passed, and they saw the black mountain, already silted up on the beach. Upon closer inspection, it was indeed a huge whale, its cries like the bellowing of a cow. Because a fish out of water has no power to exert, they hired workers to drag the fish closer to the shore for people to see. It immediately caused a sensation throughout the area. To see the end of its fins, one had to climb up a ladder. Placed on the coast for a long time, it had already developed a stench. Its meat was cut and butchered, but it was too stinky to eat. They boiled its oil for lamp fuel. It was said that someone took its belly out, and there were many gold and silver utensils inside, and its shoulder blades were said to resemble stone mortars.

Young Master Wang 254

— Yu Renmei

In this column, Mr. Zhao Ziming and the Fisherman of the East Sea have successively introduced Mr. Wang, his wife, and Miss Wang. What is missing is a Young Master Wang.

This Young Master Wang was extremely intelligent and eloquent from a young age. His apple-like face was set with lively eyes, and his lips were as red as if young girls had applied rouge. Therefore, Mr. Wang and his wife loved him as the apple of their eye.

However, although Young Master Wang was beautiful on the outside and intelligent on the inside, he simply did not like books. Mr. Wang fully intended to teach his son all the knowledge he had accumulated, so that he could "be promoted and make a fortune" and "bring glory to his family" in the future. But unexpectedly, when Young Master Wang opened a book, he kept saying "I'm dizzy." Not only did he dislike books so much, but he also called his father a "bookworm." When Mr. Wang saw him like this, he couldn't help but burst into thunderous anger. With a shout, he ordered his son to kneel in front of the ancestral hall, gritted his teeth, and began to whip him. But when Mrs. Wang saw the situation, she immediately jumped up in a rage, with tears in her eyes, scolding, "You old fool, we don't want him to take the imperial examination, why force him to read this damn thing? We are both old now, and all that's left is this bit of flesh and blood. If you force him to death, who will I rely on in the future!" Mr. Wang couldn't answer a word.

From then on, Young Master Wang became increasingly dissolute. All day long, he went with a group of hooligan youths to visit prostitutes, flirted with women, and from time to time, he became addicted to opium, his spirit becoming increasingly weakened, far from what it used to be.

When Mr. Wang and his wife saw their son so unsuccessful, they finally became depressed and unhappy and passed away one after another. It is said that when Mr. Wang and Mrs. Wang passed away, Young Master Wang was actually in a brothel, having fun with a group of prostitutes. Moreover, Young Master Wang didn't care about anything about the funeral arrangements, all of which were handled by relatives. At the same time, the family property was also seized completely. From then on, Young Master Wang gradually became short of money and had no way to borrow money. Finally, he became a beggar.

When Young Master Wang thought of the past, it was like a "Yellow Millet Dream."

Four Northeast Company Commanders 255

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Seventeen: Who Can Be Without Feelings, Family Thoughts Are Ash; Morale of Soldiers, Not厭詐; Bold Words Strengthen Military Hearts

Our troops, upon reaching the defensive area, will immediately receive their pay, and during the Mid-Autumn Festival in August, we can all have a good time. Once we start moving, we won't have to deduct food expenses. Whatever the pay is, that's what's left. Besides, as soldiers, if we only seek comfort, stationed somewhere, hoping not to move an inch for the rest of our lives, where will we find a chance to advance? Those who have reached the rank of battalion commander or higher, who hasn't endured a period of hardship? So this time, moving to Eastern Hebei is a good opportunity for us. It depends on each person's fortune. No one can say for sure who will have the chance to become an official and get rich. This is all talk that should only be said by those who have abandoned their military duties, but these soldiers took it as an absolute truth, and every one of them beamed with joy. They didn't seem as anxious as the company commanders, who were afraid of fighting foreign soldiers. Zhao Ziqiang saw that his own speech had gained some power, so he said to the soldiers: "This morning, everyone can write letters home. After this afternoon, I'm afraid there won't be any more opportunities." After speaking, he assigned several tasks to the platoon leaders and left. This was all well and good, but the company commander immediately became busy. Of his three platoon leaders, two had families. Both of them wanted to borrow a bag of flour from the company commander to support their families. The sergeant quartermaster, who was the closest to the company commander, also wanted to borrow a few dollars to pay his debts. Because the shopkeepers in several stores, hearing that the army was suddenly leaving, couldn't collect their debts and were crying. People's hearts are made of flesh, how could they completely ignore them? So they also came to discuss with the company commander, asking him to give them some money. Although the soldiers couldn't borrow whole dollars or whole bags of flour, they each had their own difficulties. The first was the company commander's order to write letters. Everyone could write a letter home. The stationery and envelopes were not a problem; they could be found at the company headquarters. But the five-cent stamp for regular mail, a full five cents in silver dollars, they didn't know where to find it. There was no way around it; they had to ask the company commander for help with this trivial matter. (223)

Wherever My Footsteps Lead

Homecoming Trilogy 256

— Bibo

A Badge is a Half-Price Ticket? The train from Shanghai North Station to Qigu Yunmeng had just passed Zhenru when two ticket inspectors walked in, wearing black serge uniforms and peaked caps with gold emblems. It was just like what Mr. Cui Wanquiu described in his novel "New Road," where the Japanese called them conductors. Indeed, Chinese people can never be as hypocritically polite as the Japanese, saying, "Excuse me, may I see your ticket?" But compared to before, when they were always followed by three or four armed military police carrying box cannons, this feeling was much better. Across from me sat two officials from the capital's government offices (or perhaps officials, because I didn't ask, so I couldn't be sure). The ticket inspector took their tickets and looked at them, but they were half-price tickets. He said, "Please take out your badge and show me the symbol." One of the plump ones took out a round badge with blue and gold lettering from his pocket. The ticket inspector verified that it was correct, punched the ticket, and returned it to him. Another gentleman in a Western suit fumbled for a long time but couldn't find it. He said, "I forgot to bring it with me." The ticket inspector said, "That is the order from the department. Without a badge, no matter who it is, they must pay the full fare according to the regulations." That gentleman in the Western suit was also very polite and did not resist because they were not escorted by armed soldiers. He took out a five-yuan Central Bank note from his wallet and paid the difference. I didn't bother to ask the ticket inspector if this badge was only valid for military, political, or railway agencies in the capital. If anyone could pay half price with a government badge, then the railway department's revenue budget would seem to have to be slightly discounted.

▲ Slapping the Bed Frame and Calling for Happiness Jia Le went to the Boxue Hospital in Tianci Village to visit his sister-in-law, and he insisted that I accompany him. I agreed readily because I also wanted to go to my friend Xiao Qing's house. Who knew that when he entered the patient's room, he suddenly felt a surge of illusory fantasies, and the smell of medicine hit him, and his mind suddenly lost control of himself. At that time, because I didn't enter the ward, I was talking to my brother-in-law in the downstairs living room. He happened to poke his head out to look at me, and just as he turned the corner, a nurse walked out. In his eyes, he felt a flash of white, and his heart couldn't help but skip a beat. In his complicated confusion, he was actually frightened. He woke up jumping throughout the night. He and I have always been comrades who advocated breaking superstitions and did not believe in gods or ghosts. This time, however, he couldn't help but think of "slapping the bed frame and calling for happiness." I couldn't do it, so I specially asked my mother-in-law to do it. Sure enough, it was effective. After calling for happiness, he slept soundly until dawn. This is probably a psychological effect, right? I am not promoting superstition here because the fact is so strange! I wrote it down, treating it as a form of hypnosis or mental telepathy. Then this kind of hypnosis is indeed our national essence and not some trick invented in the West.

▲ Ode to Pig Oil Cake White sugar rose pig oil cake, and spiced tea eggs and dried tofu, are also part of the three-part food journey for travelers. However, pig oil cake is only available at Suzhou Station, and not at other stations or on the trains. Because it is a specialty of Suzhou Station, I paid special attention to it while waiting for the train. A middle-aged man with a long, thin face was squatting down, taking care of his business—pig oil cake. First, he arranged the unheated cake pieces in a circle on a basket lined with lead and buried with a stove underneath. Then, he gradually baked them in rows of five on the heated lead. A sweet aroma was enough to make hungry travelers salivate. After they were baked, he would push the old and bring forth the new, replacing them with a row of cold ones, just like training new soldiers. If customers were not enthusiastic, he would remove the fuel from under the pot, lifting the lead and using a pair of iron chopsticks to clamp out the burning charcoal in the stove. Or, because he didn't need a strong fire for the time being, he would clamp a small, round, perforated iron plate on the edge of the stove, covering it to flatten the heat for five minutes. But at this time, the ruthless wind from the wilderness blew, scattering the white ash from the stove and spreading it on top of the pig oil cake, as if adding a lot of pepper. Because the colors were indistinguishable, there was no noticeable situation for customers to see, so his pig oil cake business was still not bad. Suddenly, he frowned, lifted the basket to the edge of the platform, jumped into the wilderness of the tracks, pulled down his pants and relieved himself! At the same time, he turned his head and stared at the basket, to prevent unscrupulous people from stealing his cake. After a while, he jumped back onto the platform. Just then, a child came up with seven copper coins in his hand to buy a cake from him. He didn't wipe his hand that had just been relieving himself, stretched out five fingers, picked up a piece, and gave it to the child. The child happily stuffed it into his mouth and chewed. This is called "what the eye doesn't see, the heart doesn't grieve"!

— Wu Yan

▲ New York Silk Prices Rise Continuously, Local American Silk Merchants, such as Lan Lebi & Co., received a telegram from New York yesterday morning, stating that since President Luo took measures to increase prices, the US exchange rate has stabilized, and the silk market has seen a surge in buying from hoarders, causing silk prices to rise sharply. The standard silk price has risen by over 0.1 US dollars per pound in three days, equivalent to a 40 yuan increase per dan in Chinese currency. Market sentiment has been boosted as a result.

▲ Rayon Sales Remain Sparse, With a Weak Foreign Exchange Rate and Firm Rayon Prices, only 15 boxes of No. 1 and No. 2 Hongyu and Lan Ning brands were shipped yesterday by local silk factories, with prices ranging from 179.5 yuan to 156.75 yuan net.

▲ American Firms Take the Opportunity to Purchase Factory Silk, The New York raw silk market has seen rising silk prices due to the American government's efforts to raise prices. Shanghai American firms have taken the opportunity to purchase factory silk, but manufacturers are reluctant to hold onto their large inventory, causing the B-grade white factory silk to be purchased by Lan Lebi and others at a stable price of 80 bales.

Foreign Tea Market Gradually Becomes Sparse 278

Yesterday, the local foreign tea market saw a decline in transactions. English firms, such as Jinlong, Xiehe, and major foreign firms, have exhausted their inventories of tea from Tunxi, Wudong, and other areas that are sold together, and are preparing to close down. In addition to packing and shipping teas purchased in previous months, they have no intention of buying any green tea for the time being. Yesterday, only Tongfu, Duder, and Yingfa and other firms bought 197 boxes of Zhenmei, Zhenmei, and Xiamu teas, with Zhenmei priced at 178 yuan at the top, Xiamu at 62 yuan, and Zhenmei at 40 yuan, all unchanged from before.

North and South Goods: Wuye Branches Arrive After a Long Interruption 279

Although there are fewer Wuye branches produced in Zhangzhou this year, the price is still relatively cheap. Due to disagreements over land prices, there has been a shortage of supply for a long time. It is now heard that a new batch will arrive soon, and it is planned to increase the price by 1-2 yuan based on the previous price. The higher-quality goods are priced at 22 yuan, and are currently being quoted. It is estimated that a decision will be made after the samples are seen.

Sugar Market: Local Refined White Sugar Falls by Another 0.15 Jiao 280

Yesterday, the sugar market remained weak due to sluggish trading. The guild's marked price for No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar was rumored to have been quoted at 21.2 yuan in the after-hours market the night before, down 0.1 jiao. Yesterday, the original price was still quoted, but there were no buyers, indicating that the weakness had not ended. No. 20 medium granulated white sugar was quoted at 20.65 yuan, with no transactions. Dutch red NT mark was 16.3 yuan, and ordinary was 16.2 yuan, down 0.2 jiao from before. Taikoo Sugar B mark was down 0.1 jiao to 21.3 yuan. Bowl green re-exported goods were quoted at 4.9 yuan, excluding tax. China, Guohua, and Zhenji local refined white sugar all fell by 0.15 jiao, with No. 1 at 20 yuan, No. 2 at 19.8 jiao, No. 3 at 19.6 jiao, and No. 4 at 19.4 jiao. Zhenji No. 5 was 19.2 jiao, China top grade was 20.6 jiao, and Zhenyu refined white sugar A mark was 20 yuan. The remaining BCD marks were each reduced by 0.2 jiao. Chaozhou groups quoted over 200 bags of Chaoqing, with the top grade at 15.75-15.7 jiao, and the next grade at 14.75-14.6 jiao. Jianbang groups increased the price of Wufu white ice sugar according to customer requests, but various firms were still eating the original price and have not yet made a transaction.

Metals: American Tinplate Ships 2,000+ Boxes 281

Yesterday, American tinplate saw a significant improvement in trading. A total of 2,300-2,400 boxes of iron were shipped, mostly to local can factories. Spot goods were scarce, with prices varying by 0.2-0.3 yuan depending on the standard. 90-pound goods with packing slips were estimated at 16.8 yuan, while goods without packing slips were quoted at 16.3 yuan. 100-pound goods with packing slips were quoted at 18 yuan, while goods without packing slips were quoted at 17.5 yuan. 200-pound double-connected goods with packing slips were estimated at 38 yuan, while goods without packing slips were quoted at 36.5 yuan. 200-pound company iron was quoted at 29 yuan. The most active trading was in 90-pound goods with packing slips. Overseas prices have been rising steadily in recent days, and the local market atmosphere has improved.
