Shen Bao National Goods Weekly

Contributions

Talking About Business Acumen 282

— Yang Mang

▲ Articles Require Skillful Management to Achieve Success

In this year of national goods promotion, the market is sluggish. People generally feel that their purchasing power is weak. Coupled with the relentless promotion of foreign goods, doing business is as difficult as climbing to the heavens. We, who are engaged in the national goods industry, must, in addition to studying the refinement of products and reducing costs, naturally study business acumen to make sense. Moreover, doing business must not be a rigid process. For example, in the past, the enemies of national goods were generally said to be only imported goods. However, after increasing import taxes, implementing place-of-origin labeling regulations, and implementing anti-dumping taxes, there are two new enemies: foreign goods that evade taxes and factories established by foreigners in China. We should prepare early.

The autumn wind is strengthening, and the mooncake era has passed. Boss Xian is also busy. We occasionally talk with Xian about business acumen and unexpectedly get a fascinating lesson from Xian, which is well worth introducing.

Xian said: Doing mooncake business for the Mid-Autumn Festival is like writing a great article. Celebrities can hire ghostwriters to write articles, but I have to use my own heart and pen. Before the Mid-Autumn Festival, I first have to draft a basic plan in my mind. How to arrange, how to describe, how to contrast, and how to structure, all require careful design and research before I can write a good and outstanding article. Doing mooncake business is really not easy: If you make too much, you can't sell it, and the store regrets it. If you make too little, people can't buy it, and they curse you to death. To be perfectly balanced, it depends on our ability to write articles. During these few days of the Mid-Autumn Festival, we are really at the crucial moment of writing articles, and we don't relax at all. Every day, I have five people guarding my command post, paying attention at all times and being careful every step of the way. One is in charge of advertising, one is in charge of external investigation, one is in charge of store investigation, one is in charge of factory manufacturing, and one is in charge of statistical research. For example, if the external investigator comes back and reports that lotus seed paste is the best-selling mooncake in all stores this year, then the store will prepare more lotus seed paste mooncakes. The factory will rush to produce them. The statistician will immediately report the findings separately and ask all departments to pay attention. The advertiser will also change methods and be original. As for me, I will respond in the middle, pointing left and right. On the evening of the Mid-Autumn Festival, I calculate the output, and it is just right, neither too much nor too little. This article is well submitted, and everyone's heart will be relieved. Do you think it's clever? It turns out that doing business should be like this, especially doing a one-time business. In general, most businesses are one-time, trendy clothing is one-time, modern clothing is one-time, any kind of commodity, when it first comes out, is one-time, but you must not be careless, only thinking about making money to ruin your own business and reduce the buyer's trust. In the end, you still suffer yourself. Tell me, how much good is there?

I think Xian's words have research and adoption value for national goods leaders in order to promote their careers.

National Goods Talks

Controlled Production and Developing National Goods 283

— Xuan Wan

Following the wild waves of the global economic panic, the rising tide of "controlled economy" is also surging before us. Currently, the chorus praising it reaches the clouds, and it can be said that it has become a unanimous opinion across the country. However, we must understand that the origin of this new term is not an empty theory but a real entity built on society. Its most important part is "controlled production," with the aim of advancing the national goods production industry through the most rationalized planning and control, ensuring the simultaneous increase of production and consumption, equal distribution, improved production methods and national living standards, and striving to prevent the import of foreign goods, so as to lead the national economy to the safest and most consolidated path.

Therefore, "controlled economy," in a narrow sense, can perhaps also be called "controlled production." Its most important purpose is nothing more than to seek government assistance and industry coordination for the national goods production industry, to develop the entire industry through the most rationalized planning and implementation, and at the same time, to strive to eliminate its business contradictions and conflicts, and to achieve a balance in all aspects of production and sales. From the previous unplanned production, it moves into the stage of planned "controlled production." In this reality and process, we can use the previous situation as a mirror for the present.

In recent years, the national goods production industry, although it has been vigorous and has made considerable progress and achievements, has always been due to the privatization of our country's commercial system. Most of them adopt "free economy" to seek the development of individual enterprises. Although there are occasionally joint business organizations, they can never maintain their normal state, and eventually disintegrate and fall apart, each seeking its own interests. Thus, industries engage in infighting and price-cutting competition, presenting a bad situation in society. In our country's industry, which is still in its infancy and backward in production, can it withstand the onslaught of storms and think of changing it?

We must deeply understand that our country is a country with backward production. The ratio of production volume to consumption volume is only two to five. Therefore, at present, the advancement of the national goods industry and the people's need for industrial products are absolutely proportional. However, in the past, due to our lack of planning and distribution, all industries were crowded into one corner and competed, and failed. What we urgently need in the future is how to balance supply and demand, adapt production and sales, and solve the problem of regional distribution. How to give accurate regulations based on its historical and geographical relationship, and popularize it throughout the vast and populous country, so that national goods factories will have no panic of overproduction, and the people will have no shame of replacing national goods with foreign goods due to the lack of national goods. Everything that should be promoted and reformed can be hoped for in the success of "controlled production."

National Crisis and National Goods 284

— Hu Liwen

This year is a year of national crisis, and also a year of national goods, as some people have already discussed in newspapers. What I want to say here is the connected relationship between national crisis and national goods:

National goods companies are posting large advertisements saying: "With such a national crisis, Chinese people should use Chinese goods!" The general bourgeois ladies and young ladies do not know there is a national crisis at all: and they all have a mindset that it is embarrassing to wear Chinese goods. Therefore, although the company's advertisements are posted so large, they do not even glance at them.

As for those poor people, due to the national crisis, the social depression, and the economic decline, it is very difficult for them not to feel hungry all day long. When their clothes are old and torn, they can only make do with them. Even if national goods cloth is cheap enough to buy a bolt for a penny, they cannot afford it!

In this way, national goods are unsalable due to the national crisis!

But, strangely, in this time of national crisis, when Chinese goods are so unsalable, foreign goods have unexpectedly become very popular and sold especially well. This is not a lie, and there is no need to talk about the past. This month's newspapers, as long as you are willing to flip through them, you will definitely find many examples of foreign goods being dumped. Alas! The national crisis has caused the unsalability of national goods, but it has also increased the sales of foreign goods. I really don't know what is in the hearts of the Chinese people?

If this continues, if the national crisis in China increases in the future, the market will be full of foreign goods, and national goods stores will have to close down!

National Goods Discussion

Several Preconditions for Preventing the Import of Foreign Goods 285

— Xiao Bai

Indeed, it goes without saying that the result of foreign goods dumping will inevitably lead to a sharp increase in import surplus and the decline of national production, the outflow of money and the decline of industry and commerce. If it is a spreading trend, then, what the wild waves reach, in the fastest period, will immediately reveal the bankruptcy of finance and the exhaustion of finance. Its dangerousness is enough to put the national economy to death.

However, the past facts are that the market state of our country in recent years has responded to the above-mentioned phenomenon, and has entered this most serious stage. It can be said that every imperialist who has entered the hall and entered the room is thinking of using economic "magic medicine" to invade, seeking market monopoly, scheming against each other, making themselves the cleaver and us the fish and meat. The arrival of foreign goods is like mercury spilling on the ground, penetrating everywhere, until it reaches remote rural areas, without leaving anything behind. As a result, the import surplus has revealed an unprecedented huge number, which is something that makes us very heartbroken.

Although promoting national goods and revitalizing industry and commerce has become the mantra of the whole country, speaking with one voice and with consistent calls, and considerable achievements have indeed been made in its past efforts and future arrangements, which is deeply gratifying, we still don't understand that the customs estimates for the import of foreign goods are always higher day by day, and the huge numbers are enough to make us tremble with fear. In my humble opinion, there are probably the following three reasons, and we have to bring them up for discussion in order to remove obstacles:

1. Tariff Issues: In the current autumn of fierce commercial warfare, all countries in the world have strict barriers, and there is no way to enter. However, our country, due to the fact that it could not control its tariffs in the past, allowed invasion. Even now, the tax revenue is very low, and there is no anti-dumping tax.

2. Preferential Treatment for Foreign Businesses in China: Foreign businesses set up factories in the mainland, using their abundant capital, complete equipment, and taking advantage of our country's low wages and exemption from donations and taxes. Their products naturally affect our industry, which is still in its infancy.

3. Shipping Issues: Our country allows all countries to freely navigate inland waterways, which is also enough to serve as a medium for increasing the import of foreign goods. Just look at the recent vigorous development of the business of various Japanese ships in the midst of the anti-Japanese goods movement, and you will see a good example.

Here, we deeply understand that as long as we strive to improve the production of national goods and the fundamental awakening of the public to refuse to use foreign goods, then the advancement of the national goods industry will always be thriving. However, we cannot ignore everything else too much. The above three points are what we consider to be the most important preconditions at present. If they are not adequately resolved in the shortest possible time, then I am afraid that the general public, especially the general national goods manufacturers, will be like looking at the clouds in a severe drought, and hoping for its early success. The problem of "preventing the import of foreign goods" will never have a thorough solution and realization.

Women and National Goods

How Women Can Promote National Goods 286

— Yang Xieli

In 1929, the total amount of Japanese goods imported into China was 306,930,000 Customs Taels. I have carefully analyzed it, and roughly speaking, non-productive goods (consumer goods) accounted for 70% of the total, and the goods that women often buy accounted for more than 43% of the total non-productive goods. Although it is uncertain whether a small part of this 43% is jointly purchased by men and women, the number actually exceeds more than half of the non-productive goods, which is really amazing. The high number of foreign goods used by women is evident from this.

Why do women buy so many foreign goods? There are probably no more than the following two reasons: (1) Young women are vain and fashionable! Loving beauty is originally the nature of young women, but their "vanity" is too great and their "fashion desire" is too strong. They worship extravagance, admire modernity, and compete to use foreign goods for all clothing and decorations to show off: the higher the value, the more it seems to show their wealth. Thus, daughters of wealthy families compete for novelty and beauty, and promote it from above; while daughters of ordinary families also admire its beauty, follow suit, and try their best to imitate it, almost considering that non-imported goods are not fashionable, and not using foreign goods is not enough to be considered modern. Even if the country can be destroyed and the family can be broken, not being fashionable and modern is not allowed! This is the first reason. (2) Older women lack patriotism and discernment: Because education is relatively unpopular and the education system is poor in our country, women have a very weak concept of the country, especially older women. Moreover, they do not often go out except to buy things, and do not pay much attention to the types of foreign goods. When buying, they only choose cheap, clever, and beautiful things, so they are most easily exploited by unscrupulous merchants, and often buy foreign goods without even knowing it. This is the second reason for buying more foreign goods.

Judging from the above two reasons, women's purchase of more foreign goods is not without reason. If we want to promote national goods, women's responsibility is really great.

Moreover, the so-called national goods naturally include clothing, food, and use. According to Chinese customs, men manage outside affairs and women manage internal affairs. The clothing materials, socks, children's clothing, food, and all daily necessities used in the family are mostly purchased by women. If women can really promote national goods, its effect will be above that of men.

Then how can women promote national goods? Roughly speaking, it can be divided into three categories: (1) Promote thrift: Excessive consumption and waste, and excessive trends towards luxury, are contrary to the path of life. For example, clothing, which originally only seeks cleanliness and comfort, does not need to be very beautiful and luxurious. National goods are already available, and women may as well take thrift as a virtue and strive to promote national goods: on the one hand, it can reduce the family burden, and on the other hand, it can serve the country! (2) Change concepts: "Fashion" and "modern" originally have no fixed standards, but are just a trend of the times. Looking back decades ago, women all considered small feet to be fashionable. Once this trend is reformed, if women still bind their feet, it will become a joke. Therefore, if women in the knowledge community can take the lead, purchase and use national goods, change their vision, and regard using national goods as fashionable, it may not be impossible to change customs and habits. (3) Pay attention to identification: Women can carefully check their daily necessities, and ask people who understand what they cannot identify. See how many foreign goods you have used, so that you can be vigilant in the future. Or combine with several families to collect foreign goods and use them as specimens for public viewing, reducing the opportunity for the public to be fooled.

Some people say: Unscrupulous merchants, in order to cater to the purchasing desires of many women, disregard the survival and interests of the country and purchase foreign goods. I think this is not an exaggeration: because from the principles of economics, the needs of the buyers are the main conditions that determine the market and the quantity of production. If women, who are in the dominant position of consumers and buyers, can reduce or eliminate the need for foreign goods, then unscrupulous merchants will definitely lament their miscalculation.

Now, there are indeed many women participating in social activities and making practical efforts for the country. In this matter, I think they can certainly show their strength even more!

Come! Let's All Arm Ourselves with National Cloth! 287

— Nanguo Jiaren

What do you think of thin clothes in late autumn? The national territory has been lost for a long time; How can we sleep on firewood and taste gall? May everyone arm themselves with national cloth!

Recently, a friend of mine came back from overseas. He came in from the South Gate (Hong Kong, Guangzhou), passed through the Southeast Gate (Shantou, Xiamen), then entered the East Gate (Shanghai), and entered the newly built main hall (the capital). He was very happy looking here and looking there. Because I had been separated from him for a long time and we had reunited, I opened my mouth and asked him: "You have been abroad for several years. Come back and take a look at your old home. The entire field in the Northeast has been offered to the domineering eastern neighbor as unmortgaged land. Seeing the east-wearing and west-wearing in the country, do you feel that the country will perish without a day?"

That friend gave me a blunt answer: "I think China will not perish, but the nation has the atmosphere of rejuvenation. To prove this, there are more modern men and women wearing suits and student uniforms than before. Comrades in long gowns who bow respectfully seem to be gradually decreasing compared to before."

I smiled in disappointment and said: "You are wrong! The comrades wearing short clothes, especially suits, consume almost all foreign goods. These treasures are adding capital to foreign factories and increasing the naval, land, and air force power of imperialism to oppress our weak nation. Where is the atmosphere of national prosperity? It is simply the vanguard of national destruction."

That friend, without waiting for me to finish speaking, gritted his teeth and explained: "Short clothes are the clothing of the working class. No matter what, they are always more convenient than long gowns and robes similar to cassocks. If we want national rejuvenation, we must invigorate every citizen; then we must learn from King Zhao Wuling and wear foreign clothes instead of long gowns. Now the national cloth products are thriving. As long as everyone uses national goods to make short clothes, then can't both form and spirit be improved?"

"Among the young people in suits I have seen everywhere, in addition to a few university professors, rich fashionable young men, and administrative personnel wearing foreign suits on lantern frames, many more practical young people are happy to use national cloth to make short clothes. As for the uniforms of students in various schools, that goes without saying."

"As for the qipao materials of modern women, most of them love to use national products. Women who imitate suits can even be said to be a manifestation of 'when the country is about to prosper, there must be auspicious omens'. I have seen many foreign women, whether old or young, ugly or beautiful, almost all like to buy Chinese silk fabrics and embroidered products as fashionable clothes. Foreign men's clothes pay attention to 'stiffness', while women's clothes pay attention to 'lightness'. There are many national goods stores abroad that make money by relying on foreign modern women. If the new era women in China all learn from Western beauties and compete to use national silk and cotton fabrics to make modern clothes, wouldn't they be directly consuming the surplus money of their husbands or parents, and indirectly promoting national goods there?"

"In short, the national cloth arming movement is more practical and effective than all slogans and all declarations of important people!"

Hearing what he said made sense, I and my "Prime Minister" and "Little Adou" armed ourselves with national cloth together.

Rural Areas and National Goods

The Countryside and the National Goods Movement 288

— Huang Yingdai

▲Everyone Go to the Countryside to Promote National Goods

In this year of national goods, the slogan of promoting national goods has almost been shouted all over China. However, we feel that the amount of publicity seems to be very different between cities and the countryside. In general, those who bear the mission of promoting national goods are mostly engaged in the national goods movement in cities, but they have abandoned the mission of going to the countryside to publicize it. They do not take it upon their shoulders.

We feel that the hearts of the people in the city have already died. In China, no matter which city it is, the more lively it is, the more foreign goods are flooding it. If you don't believe it, look at the city of Greater Shanghai, the so-called Paris of the Far East. The number of young men in suits, young women in fancy clothes, cars coming and going, and locomotives speeding is undoubtedly more than in all the cities in China.

Shanghai is a major base for exclusive sales of foreign goods. If Shanghai is destroyed, China's imports will be reduced by at least more than half. Foreign goods and civilization have become directly proportional to each other. In the eyes of people in the city, not wearing a suit or riding in a car seems to be unworthy of being called a civilized person. In this city filled with foreign air, those who promote national goods are just publicizing every day, and those who buy foreign goods are just going to buy foreign goods. And the effect of the publicity, although not completely lost, is also minimal.

Therefore, I think that rather than promoting the national goods movement in the city, it is better to first go to the countryside to publicize it. Although in the countryside, due to different environments and different positions, whether foreign goods have invaded and how foreign goods are consumed, we cannot treat every village the same. But no matter what, the consumption of foreign goods in the countryside is definitely not as large as that in the city, which is an undeniable problem.

Moreover, in fact, like the villages that are closer to the city, they have been somewhat urbanized under the influence of the environment. Therefore, the invasion of foreign goods has also occupied a part of the power. But the older farmers may not have the need to use foreign goods for clothing, food, and housing. As for the villages that are farther away from the city and where transportation is inconvenient, foreign goods are extinct.

As long as we walk into a rural village, we will see the elders in the village. They wear felt hats on their heads, old cloth clothes on their bodies, cloth socks, and cloth-soled shoes. Everything on their bodies is national goods. The houses they live in are also built by Chinese craftsmen, not foreign houses. The utensils in the house are also mostly national goods. The white rice and fish and meat they eat are even more local products. Therefore, I think these people are the practitioners of promoting national goods. Everything we see in the countryside is completely different from that in the city, without any foreign air.

However, to say it again, the clothes, food, and housing needed by the general elders in the countryside are all national goods. However, recently, the younger farmers, because they have been influenced by the big cities and small cities, also have a tendency to like foreign goods. Copper basin hats, silk stockings, leather-soled shoes, and some wider serge and Gabardine robes, also have a few daily necessities, and they are also intent on luxury and buying foreign goods. Therefore, the power of foreign goods in the countryside is also expanding with the wheel of time.

China is a country based on agriculture. Among the 400 million compatriots, farmers account for the majority. Therefore, the area occupied by rural areas is also wider than the area occupied by cities. Now, foreign goods are still in the initial invasion of the countryside. If the power of foreign goods in the countryside expands in the future, so that the rural areas in China are invaded by foreign goods, then we believe that the number of foreign goods imported each year will be hundreds of times more than today. The future is an extremely dangerous thing.

At this critical moment, while the power of foreign goods in the countryside has not yet been deeply rooted, we can just go to the countryside to vigorously publicize and promote national goods, so that the general farmers know that buying foreign goods is a suicidal policy and is very dangerous. Explain the various interests and harms, so that all farmers do not use foreign goods. Because there are relatively few people in the countryside who use foreign goods, it is easier to publicize and promote national goods. The effect must be greater than in the city. Therefore, I think that to promote national goods and resist foreign goods, we should first publicize in the countryside.

Enamel Utensils and the Countryside 289

— He Gongxing

Enamel products are a kind of durable goods. Their categories, such as washbasins, food baskets, and rice bowls and teacups, are especially necessary for daily life. According to the principles of social economy, it is in line with the economic principles for people to prepare necessary supplies. Now, if there are durable necessary supplies to choose from, then their contribution to the social economy of a country is even greater. This is not only a matter of promoting national goods.

Now, we advocate the use of national goods and loudly proclaim the slogan of national goods penetrating into the countryside. Unfortunately, in recent years, the rural economy has declined and the purchasing power of farmers is extremely weak. This is a national problem as a whole, and there is a real need for active relief. However, whether national goods should be sold to the countryside at this time, and whether the countryside needs national goods, are preconditions that those who are responsible for promoting national goods should pay attention to.

Today's proponents of saving the country all advocate a frugal movement. The frugality of Chinese farmers can be said to be the best in the world. Not to mention the distant past, but the farmers in Jiangsu and Zhejiang still mostly wear coarse cloth clothes and burn vegetable oil lamps. Some even still use stone to make fire. Even the rural farmers in the Pudong area still mostly use wooden basins to wash their faces. Other things can be known from this. The object of promoting national goods is to refuse to use foreign goods. Today, farmers do not have much need for foreign goods. Although it is because of the lack of purchasing power, they do not need much anyway. Now, if we want national goods to penetrate into the countryside, we should also make a choice. If we are not careful, we will go from promoting national goods to promoting luxury. This is also a major research problem. Then, what kind of national goods should be deeply rooted in the countryside today? It is none other than enamel products.

I am not just advertising for enamel factories. Enamel is a durable product, and most of its products are needed by farmers. The same washbasin, if you buy a wooden one, you can't get it for less than four or five dimes. If you change to a small enamel basin, two or three dimes are enough. And it is light, clean, and beneficial to hygiene. It is not worth saving a dime to buy an enamel rice bowl. I have seen farmers using clumsy porcelain bowls, which are only worth a hundred or so coins each, but once they are dropped, they are useless. Enamel rice bowls will not break even if they are dropped a hundred times. No matter how they are used, they can be used for three years. As for using porcelain ones, at least ten or twenty or thirty of them will be used in three years. The ratio of one to twenty is complete. This is the fact, not a clever exaggeration. For other things, such as drying powder, there are enamel round and square plates. For storing seeds, there are enamel large and small pots. They cannot be invaded by moisture, and insects and mice cannot harm them. Ask about the price, and it is lower than bamboo and wooden utensils. Almost all kinds of enamel utensils meet the needs of rural utensils. As for the enamel warehouse basket, it is especially a wonderful product for delivering meals on the fields when farmers are busy with farming. Bean soup and vegetable soup are displayed separately. Sitting around and starting to eat, the heat is still there. It is not only its joy that is also. Therefore, in the future, the countryside will become more economical and frugal because of the use of enamel utensils. Enamel utensils will become more developed and cheaper because they penetrate into the countryside. I can't help but shout loudly: Long live the countryside! Long live enamel utensils!

Observation Notes

A Visit to the Zhanghua Woolen Textile Factory 290

— Wu Yiheng, Chen Shuying

▲Motivation for the Visit　Our country's woolen fabric market has long been monopolized by foreign merchants. It is estimated that the annual outflow of money is always more than 30 million [dollars]. Fortunately, recently, Mr. Liu Hongsheng, a Chinese national, established the Zhanghua Woolen Textile Factory, which emerged as a dark horse. The fabrics it produces are almost superior to imported goods in terms of quality, and the prices are low, which has led to a rapid rise in its reputation. Its various products sell quickly without needing to be promoted. It is expected that in a few years, it will be able to keep foreign goods out of the country. We have long heard of the name of Zhanghua and are eager to see its internal workings to understand the general situation of our country's emerging industries. However, because we lacked a familiar introduction and sufficient time, our long-cherished wish was difficult to fulfill, which was a pity.

▲Invitation from the Assistant Manager　After the start of the summer vacation, Mr. Xu Peixing of our school received a letter of invitation from Mr. Wu Bokuan, the assistant manager of the factory, asking us to visit. A group of 23 of us boarded the factory's private launch at the New Customs Wharf at 9:00 AM on September 17th to begin our trip. During this visit, we were treated with great hospitality and given detailed explanations of the factory's operations, allowing us to tour the entire factory within two hours. From raw materials to finished products, we collected a sample of each to use as educational material for production. We benefited greatly, thanks to Mr. Wu. Now, we will record what we learned during the visit, regarding the textile process of various woolen fabrics, as follows, which we believe will also be of interest to people in the country.

▲Textile Raw Materials　The raw materials used by the factory are described below in terms of their types, sources, uses, and quantities used:

A. Types

(1) Wool (sheep)

(2) Camel hair

(3) Cotton yarn (for camel down)

B. Sources (Wool)

(1) Domestic: Gansu, Xining, Hunan, Huzhou, Shandong, Henan, Shanxi, Tibet

(2) Foreign: Australia

C. Uses

(1) High-grade woolen fabrics (overcoat cloth, riding breeches cloth, straight twill cloth, gabardine) are woven from camel hair or Shandong wool mixed with Australian wool.

(2) Medium-grade woolen fabrics (uniform cloth, coarse serge, etc.) are woven from Huzhou wool mixed with Shandong wool.

(3) Low-grade woolen fabrics (military uniform cloth, camel down, etc.) are woven with cotton yarn as the warp and Huzhou wool as the weft.

D. Quantities Used

(1) Huzhou wool is used the most.

(2) Shandong wool is second.

(3) Camel hair is third.

(4) Cotton yarn is only used for the back of camel down.

(5) Not much wool from other regions and Australian wool are currently used, but the factory plans to increase the production of high-grade woolen fabrics in the future, at which time the quantity used will increase sharply.

▲Machinery　Most of the machinery in the factory was transferred from the old Hui Weaving Factory, and most of it is made in Belgium. The newly purchased machinery is from England and France. Except for the work of sorting wool, mending, and measuring, which all rely entirely on manual labor, all other work is done entirely by machinery. In total, there are no less than 20 types of machinery in the factory, totaling over 100 machines. Broadly speaking, there are steam engines, electric motors, wool washing machines, wool drying machines, wool blending machines, wool carding machines, wool combing machines, dyeing machines, spinning machines, yarn winding machines, weaving machines, and raising machines.

▲Work Conditions

(1) Spinning

1. Sorting Wool　Sorting wool is the exclusive domain of female workers. The work relies entirely on individual experience. Each woman has a bamboo sieve in front of her and several bamboo baskets beside her. The best wool is put into the first basket. The next best is divided into the second, third, and fourth baskets. The unusable wool is called "foot wool," which is used to make coarse wool blankets and carpets.

2. Washing Wool　After the wool is sorted, it is placed in a wool washing machine for cleaning. There are five machines in total. In each wool washing machine tank, water is mixed with an appropriate amount of soap and acid, and then heated to the specified temperature to completely remove the plant matter and dirt (such as grass leaves, dust, etc.) attached to the wool, without damaging the essence of the wool fiber. After five washes, the wool is free of impurities.

3. The wool drying machine is steam-powered and has a very high temperature. The machine body is a flat, rectangular iron box divided into four compartments. After the top compartment is dried, it automatically tilts into the second compartment, then into the third and fourth compartments, and finally automatically tilts out of the box. This cycle continues endlessly. In addition, there is a drying stove and a drying cabinet. The daily output can supply the entire factory. After the wool is dried, if it is to be used for spinning and weaving natural-colored woolen serge, it is sent for carding or taken out for bleaching. Otherwise, it must go through the dyeing process.

4. Dyeing　The factory uses only high-quality dyes for dyeing. After these dyes are mixed with water and heated, they can be completely absorbed by the wool to be dyed, leaving only a tank of clear water. These dyes are expensive, but the dyed material will never fade. The dyeing tanks are used exclusively for dyeing wool and camel hair. The other square wooden tanks are used for dyeing wool yarn, wool thread, and other items. There are also constantly rotating machines used to dye woven pieces of cloth. Mr. Wu told us, "Before dyeing any wool or woolen fabrics, we must first weigh them carefully and then mix them with the appropriate amount of dye. If the proportions are not correct, the resulting color will not be as satisfactory as expected."

5. Blending Wool　After the dried wool is determined to be used for weaving what kind of woolen fabric, it must go through the wool blending process. For example, to weave high-grade woolen fabrics, Australian wool should be mixed with Shandong wool. To weave medium-grade woolen fabrics, Shandong wool should be mixed with Huzhou wool. This ensures that the material is strong and the cost is appropriate, maintaining the reputation of the products.

6. Oiling　After washing, the wool is mostly ivory-colored. If it is used directly for spinning and weaving woolen fabrics, the wool will be light and easily fly away. The resulting products will be dull and lackluster. Therefore, after blending the wool, oil must be added to the wool and stirred repeatedly to make the wool shiny and reflective. Then, when it is used for spinning and weaving woolen fabrics, the resulting products will be bright and eye-catching.

7. Carding Wool　After oiling, the wool is still mixed together, and the fibers are tightly bound. It cannot be spun into yarn unless it is carded loose.

8. Combing Wool　Each wool combing machine has three frames. The first step is to turn the wool into a thin wadding and then into a roll. After being combed by the third machine, it becomes a wool thread.

9. Spinning Yarn　After the wool is combed into threads, it is placed on a spinning machine to be spun into fine yarn. If it needs to be made into plied wool thread, it is placed on a plying machine. If it needs to be dyed, the wool yarn or wool fabric is placed on a yarn winding machine to wind it into bobbins.

10. Winding Yarn　After plying, if it is ready for sale, or if the spun yarn needs to be dyed, it must go through the yarn winding process to form skeins of yarn. There are many types of finished products, such as yarn for weaving woolen fabrics, camel down yarn, and wool yarn.

(2) Weaving

1. Preparation　Preparation work includes warping and heddling, etc.

2. Weaving Cloth　The structure of the weaving machine is roughly the same as that of ordinary silk weaving machines. However, the machine body is larger and can weave woolen fabrics with a width of seven or eight feet. Each machine is operated by two female workers. If a warp or weft thread breaks, the machine is stopped immediately to rejoin the thread, and then the machine is restarted to continue weaving. Therefore, the woven woolen fabrics rarely have broken threads from beginning to end.

(3) Finishing

1. Inspection　After the woolen fabric is woven, it is inspected. If any defects are found, they are immediately handed over to female workers for repair.

2. Mending　Mending mostly involves using tweezers to remove broken threads or using needles to repair pulled threads. However, upon close observation of the female workers on site, there were those mending broken threads, but none were found repairing pulled threads.

3. Washing Cloth　The woolen fabric taken off the machine inevitably has oil stains or dirt. Therefore, all woven woolen fabrics must be washed. During washing, the woolen fabric is suspended in the air and then gradually immersed in water. The woolen fabric in the water is agitated and shaken by boiling water, which removes the stains. This process is repeated, and soon the entire piece of woolen fabric is cleaned, and then a second piece is replaced.

4. Fulling Cloth　Fulling is done by using a machine to shrink the cloth, making the texture thicker.

5. Drying Cloth　After fulling, the cloth is not completely dry and must be placed on a cloth drying machine to dry. One end of the machine is connected to a small room about two zhang (approximately 20 feet) long, where the temperature is extremely high. The wet cloth enters the room from the machine and must be looped back and forth four or five times in the room before being hung out from the bottom of the machine. By this point, it is completely dry.

6. Raising the Nap　There are two types of machines for raising the nap. High-grade woolen fabrics are placed on a machine inlaid with plant shells (the shells resemble honeycombs and have many soft, sharp thorns on the surface, the name of which is unknown). Because the thorns are soft and sharp, the woolen fabric itself is not damaged after raising. Other lower-grade woolen fabrics, such as camel hair and military uniform cloth, are placed on a machine covered with steel wires for raising the nap. When we visited, we saw camel down being raised. When the camel down was not raised, it was as thin as terry cloth. After being raised on the raising machine three times, it not only increased in thickness several times, but the down quality was also soft, beautiful, and pleasing to the eye.

9. Shearing, Pressing, Steaming, Folding, and Measuring　After the woolen fabric is raised, it must go through many processes such as shearing, smoothing, ironing, pressing, steaming, folding, and measuring before it can be packaged. These processes are all done by machinery.

▲Development Plan　According to Mr. Wu, the following are some of the development plans that the factory is currently undertaking:

(1) Adding Night Shifts　The supply of Zhanghua products cannot meet the demand. To meet orders and reduce costs, night shifts will be started. According to the principles of scientific management and making the most of resources, there is no need for factories and machinery to rest. After adding night shifts, only an additional wage bill is incurred, while production can be doubled. In this way, the cost can be reduced, and the price can be lower, which will inevitably affect foreign goods.

(3) Purchasing New Machines　The factory's existing steam engine is expensive and inefficient. It is planned to replace all of them with electric motors soon. In addition, the factory currently lacks various machines for weaving high-grade woolen fabrics. A large batch has recently been ordered from England and will arrive soon.

Introduction to National Products

National Product: Handkerchiefs 291

— Zhen

Recently, 120 million [dollars] of our country's money flows into the hands of foreigners every year, year after year, and beautiful imported goods are imported more and more every year. As a result, the national products seen on the market are falling behind year by year. What a painful thing this is!

Many young men and women also feel sorry for this outflow of money, so they advocate national products. Thus, this year is called the "National Products Year," and everyone seems very enthusiastic. But after the five-minute enthusiasm passes, they are buying imported goods again.

The so-called modern men and women are dressed in well-tailored Western suits, and the women are dressed in modern fashions. The men often stuff a small handkerchief in a small pocket on the left side, and the women often stuff a small silk handkerchief in the middle of their silk buttons. Perhaps nine out of ten of these handkerchiefs are imported goods. It's really strange. Aren't there such handkerchiefs among our national products?

Handkerchiefs are indeed a practical item that is essential for daily use. Recently, imported handkerchiefs have flooded the market in countless numbers. If you are not careful when buying them, you may buy inferior goods, which is really a waste of money.

Now, I can introduce a genuine national product handkerchief, which is also an outstanding one among national products. It is the San Yang brand handkerchief manufactured by the Huada Handkerchief Factory, which was founded by Chinese nationals. Their raw materials are excellent, the styles are modern, and the colors are bright. Everything is comparable to imported goods. The factory is equipped with new-style machines and uses scientific manufacturing methods. The products are of good quality, so sales are expanding day by day. According to current calculations, the places that have been sold to include North China, South China, and Central China in the country, and the Nanyang Islands area abroad. Although the goods are being manufactured as quickly as possible, they are still not enough to be distributed, which also shows that our country's handkerchief industry is full of hope. I hope that all men and women compatriots in the country will quickly purchase national product handkerchiefs and not send valuable money into the hands of foreigners.

National Product: Insulated Water Bottles 292

— Geng Shang

Insulated water bottles are a daily necessity. Their effectiveness is especially noticeable in cold weather.

As long as a family has a thermos, they can have hot water to drink at any time, which is very convenient. Some people say that if the patriotism of the Chinese people could be like a thermos, keeping warm 24 hours a day, then hated foreign goods would definitely not sell so well in China. Although this is a humorous saying, it does contain profound meaning.

The weather is getting colder now! When buying thermos bottles, be sure to recognize them clearly and don't buy hated foreign goods. It is best to go to the Wuzhou Pharmacy to buy the national product "99 Thermos Bottle." This type of bottle has a beautiful style, is accurate and durable, and can be said to be superior to foreign goods. As for the words "99," it means that each piece is only sold for 9 jiao and 9 fen.

A Year's History of National Products: The National Product Cosmetics Industry (3) 293

— Ye Zhongting

(4) The Current Crisis of Cosmetics Factories

Imported cosmetics can be divided into Eastern and Western types. Eastern goods have gradually declined after repeated boycotts. Since occupying our Northeast, Chinese people have increasingly known to strive hard. Examining their sales in China, they only account for about 1% of our country's total. Western cosmetics are sold in the major cities of our country, deeply rooted and very prosperous. Although the strength of various factories is concentrated to compete with them, their popularity remains the same. This proves that the Chinese people's psychology of worshiping foreign goods is unbreakable, and this is especially true for those who are known as high-class Chinese and modern women. Foreign merchants have obtained huge profits and often use their authority of strong capital to be enemies of our Chinese factories. They usually spy on the market. If there is a fast-selling Chinese factory product, they will forcibly say that it is similar to their product and falsely accuse it of being a shadow. Therefore, the Trademark Bureau of the Ministry of Industry and the courts often have such cases. If our country's large factories are involved, they can deal with it in a just manner. However, small factories with limited funds and timidity often compromise and voluntarily destroy the disputed trademark and no longer use it. Then, foreign merchants are complacent, and our country's small factories are destroyed.

At the same time, cosmetics factories, with the purpose of making profits, often develop a morbid psychology. Knowing that Chinese people like to use foreign goods, they use foreign characters on their products and mark them with the names of foreign firms. Buyers do not examine carefully and are easily deceived. On the surface, manufacturers and sellers can make excuses to compete with foreign goods. However, examining their intentions, they have the suspicion of forgetting their ancestors. It is more accurate to say that sellers do not know how to love the country than to say that buyers do not know how to love the country.

In addition, mutual infighting among the same industry can put the future of the cosmetics industry in an irretrievable situation. It is common to see several similar products on the market for a fast-selling product. Their names, decorations, etc., are almost indistinguishable. This inside story does not need to be explained. It is obviously done by people who are greedy for profit. As a result, they lower prices to compete with each other. Eventually, the price decreases and the workmanship becomes inferior. They lose the trust of customers and then stop. This kind of psychology of seeing profit and forgetting righteousness is extremely despicable. It is absolutely not possible to forgive them by using the words "only knowing how to imitate but having no creativity." In the past, sales in Southeast Asia were over one million per year, of which Guang Sheng Hang, Sincere Company, and Wing On Enterprise Company accounted for a particularly dominant position. It is not easy to achieve such results in foreign trade. However, overseas Chinese merchants have recently become indifferent to national products. The reason is that various factories imitate each other. Their weaknesses of cutting corners and producing crudely can be concealed temporarily, but they will be exposed eventually. Therefore, this good market, which has been painstakingly managed for many years, has been destroyed by a small number of unscrupulous colleagues, and they sit back and watch as Japanese goods replace it. In our country's immature cosmetics industry, is this not extremely heartbreaking in history?

(5) Conclusion

The cosmetics industry is under the pressure of internal and external troubles, as mentioned above. If this continues and no efforts are made to progress, the future is really worrying. Therefore, today, cosmetics factories in our country urgently need to cheer up, thoroughly correct their past mistakes, unite sincerely, and coordinate their steps to prepare for a frontal impact with foreign goods. The effective steps that should be taken are to focus on improving the "quality," increasing the "quantity," lowering the "price," and opening up the "market." Chemical experts should also be hired to research how to manufacture the raw materials of cosmetics and implement them to supply various factories for application. In this way, they can no longer depend on others. Otherwise, even if imported cosmetics can disappear from China, the leak in raw materials will not be plugged, and in fact, it will still be of no help. Although there are conflicts of interest in the operations of various factories, they should all strive to improve the material itself to find a way out. There are still not many satisfactory products on the market, and there are plenty of opportunities for promotion. Do not do things that harm others and do not benefit yourself to drive yourself to depravity or even cause the entire cosmetics industry to suffer a bad influence. If the goods are of good quality and low price, Chinese people, except for a small number of the bourgeoisie who must use foreign goods to show their wealth, will be able to shift their habits as long as they know that the interests of the country are the premise. Commentators often attribute the obstruction of sales of national products to the fact that users do not know how to promote them. I think it is difficult to convince people with this statement before the products are sufficiently refined and the prices are as low as possible. Try to study the reasons why Eastern goods were overthrown in the past, and you can think about it for half the time. People are forced to act by strength. We can only resist with strength. We can only boycott with empty words or make meaningless sighs. Neither is a strong performance. If we can be down-to-earth and continue to use the strength that overthrew Eastern goods in the past and enrich it, then it will not be difficult to exclude Western goods from the territory, and national products will have a day to rise again. I hope that this arduous mission will be shouldered together with our cosmetics industry.

Page 19

Free Talk

Free Talk: An Explanation of "Humor" 294

— Wei Su

People who study world literature tell us: the French are good at wit, the Russians are good at satire, and the British and Americans are good at humor. This is probably true, as it is all limited by social conditions. Ever since Master Yutang promoted "humor," this term has become very popular, but with popularity comes crisis, just like soldiers calling themselves Buddhists, high officials suddenly wearing rosary beads, and Buddhism is about to enter Nirvana. If glibness, frivolousness, and obscenity are all labeled "humor," then it is just like "new plays" entering the "X World," and it will undoubtedly become "civilized plays."

This danger is because China has never been very humorous. There is glibness, but humor is still a long way off. The Japanese translated "humor" as "affectionate glibness," so it is different from mere "glibness," and that is why. Then, in China, can only glib articles be found? But not really. Chinese articles that think they are glib are still glib, frivolous, and obscene, and are different from true glibness. The key to this "raccoon dog swapping prince" is that the so-called serious remarks and facts in the past are mostly glib, and people are used to seeing them, gradually thinking they are normal, and then mistakenly recognize glibness as glibness.

To find glibness in China, you should not read so-called glib articles, but read so-called serious things, but you must think about it. These famous articles are readily available, such as the serious titles in newspapers, such as "Gradually Entering a Better State" and "Where is China Going," which are all like olives when chewed, with some aftertaste.

There are also some in the advertisements in newspapers. We know that there is a publication that calls itself the "new authority in the opinion world" and "says what ordinary people want to say but have not said," while at the same time "declaring a misunderstanding and expressing apologies" to another publication, but also saying that "both parties are reputable publications in the society and have no reason to attack each other." A "new authority" who is good at "misunderstandings," "misunderstands" but is "reputable," and "says what ordinary people want to say but have not said" is a misunderstanding and an apology: to not laugh at this, you must not be able to think.

There are also some in the short comments in newspapers. For example, in September, "Free Talk" published "Lost Treasures of the Art of Climbing the Dragon," which regarded marrying a rich man's daughter as one of the "arts of climbing the dragon," and soon attracted a counterattack, which began by saying: "The fox can't eat grapes, so it says the grapes are sour. He can't marry a rich wife, so he is jealous of everyone who marries a rich family. The result of jealousy is attack." You can't think about this either. Thinking about the "result" clearly shows that this author is stating that he knows that the taste of "rich wife" is sweet.

We have also seen similar wonderful articles in grand and formal official documents: and they are not caricatured, but they are originally cartoons. In "The Analects" of one year, I like to read the "Gu Xiang Zhai" column the most, such as the order of the magistrate of Yingshan County, Sichuan, prohibiting the wearing of long gowns, saying: "It must be known that clothes are enough to cover the body, why drag them back and forth, wasting cloth? And the power is weak... Considering the difficult times, what dire consequences can be imagined?" Another example is the article prohibiting women from raising male dogs in a certain place, saying: "It is found that the coexistence of female women and male dogs is not only harmful to health, but also easily leads to shameless and obscene rumors. In our country, which is a land of etiquette, it is also not allowed by custom. This is a special order to strictly prohibit... All male dogs raised by women will be beheaded without pardon, so as to rectify!" Where can a glib writer write this out of thin air?

However, the wonderful articles collected by "Gu Xiang Zhai" often tend to be bizarre (Grotesk), but glibness is not as good as plainness, and because it is plain, it is even more glib. On this standard, I recommend the "Sweet Grapes" statement.

Performance of "Roar, China!" 295

— Chen Yi

"Roar, China!" was already performed last month, but due to other matters, I missed the opportunity. Tonight is the last day and last performance of the second run, so I had to go see it no matter what.

I sat in the theater for a while before the curtain finally opened. Scene after scene passed, and I watched it all in one go.

Regarding the performance of this play, I would like to say a few words.

(1) The script. This script was written by a foreigner and has caused a sensation in theater circles around the world. Naturally, it has its value. However, is its power of expression sufficient? This is a question worth considering. When I read the script, I didn't feel it, but after watching the performance tonight, I discovered its weakness. This is partly due to the performers making slight modifications to the script, such as deleting the superstitious characters like the monk and the immortal swordsman who believe that a piece of yellow cloth can ward off bullets; the action of the university student kneeling and begging the captain; the reason for the tea boy's suicide, and so on. On the other hand, it is also due to the original author's insufficient depiction of the naked oppression of imperialism towards the people in the colonies, the cruel methods used, and the suffering of the colonized people resisting the oppression. As a result, the whole play feels loose. Perhaps because the author is a foreigner and does not fully understand the cruel situation of the Chinese people being oppressed, or perhaps because the translation of the script is not good, in short, the play does not feel very tense or profound.

(2) The technique of the performance. This can be discussed from several aspects.

A. Actors. Among the actors, the makeup of those playing foreigners is really bad, they simply don't look like foreigners. In terms of performance, only the captain and the American merchant buying cowhide were relatively better. The rest failed to show the demeanor of a foreigner, especially the women. Among the workers, the second boatman and his wife were a little better. The stoker is the most important character in the whole play, but the actor failed to fulfill the mission he shouldered in the script, and his movements were very artificial and clumsy. Only the old boatman and the boatman's old [illegible character] were passable. As for the university student, he was terrible. Originally, in the script, he was afraid when he boarded the warship, but the actor portrayed him as a brave and fearless figure. This error in characterization is probably the responsibility of the director!

B. Scenery. The scenery this time can be said to be the most magnificent on the Chinese stage. However, it still doesn't look very real. The cannons on the warship are obviously fake, the high lookout post is also very simple, the handrails and iron bars are shaky, and the cannons are connected to the lookout post, which I have never seen before. The scene of the dock in the first scene doesn't look like it at all, and the ships are completely different from the real ones. The scene of the small cigarette shop is a little better, but the door is too pretty. The dock scene is the best set, but it is still not real, and it shakes every time it is touched. Another point is that the backstage staff did not eliminate the past shortcomings and were always moving around behind the scenery.

C. Lighting. The lighting is really bad, always moving, strong, and without a specific direction. The searchlight was supposed to shine down from the lookout post, but they made it shine from the front of the lookout post. If that's not a searchlight, then what is it for? If it is said to be a searchlight from elsewhere, there is absolutely no reason for it to shine on the warship. The lighting in the small hotel is even more strange, the light from outside is stronger than the light inside. We ask, was there a moon that night? Was there a street lamp right outside the door?

(3) The overall performance and effect. The entire performance of the play can be said to be powerless. The actors' movements, expressions, and words cannot move the audience or give them a deep impression, and completely fail to produce the effect of the play. The expression of the consciousness of several different characters is also not fully revealed. It can be said that the effect of this play is only to leave people with the impression that there was such a thing, without making them understand the ferocity of imperialism and the suffering of the Chinese people.

Finally, I would like to say to the Theater Association and friends in the theater world with the utmost sincerity: please put more effort into this undertaking and expand its power so that all the people who are suffering as much as the workers in the play can see and hear it!

Bewilderment 296

— Liao Botan

Last year, also at this time of day, with the sun setting and the low murmur of falling leaves making the silence even more profound.

I walked through the dusty streets, dragging my tired legs into my house.

My house seemed shrouded in a layer of mist, and the old rooms were even more so.

My mother, looking haggard, lay on a chaise lounge, her thin, bony hand covering her forehead.

Even the slightest sound of footsteps startled her:

"Who is it?" Her voice was gentle, weak, and dim.

"It's me..." I immediately felt uneasy and sad.

"You're back?"

She sighed, seemingly falling asleep again.

Reply to "Also for Your Consideration" 297

— Feng Zhiyu

After writing an article titled "Missing Out" a few days ago, I didn't want to say anything more about "Zhuangzi and Selections of Refined Literature." The next day, I saw Mr. Shi Zhicun's "Letter to Mr. Li Liewen" on "Free Talk," which was also "for my consideration," so I will say a few more words. Because I feel that Mr. Shi's three rebuttals are all beside the point:

(1) Mr. Shi said that since "some new youths can have old ideas, and some old forms can contain new content," then the old ideas of someone like him, "a limb of the remaining subjects of the fallen dynasty," can be left unexamined, and writing ancient texts like "Zhuangzi" is also permissible. Of course, if one wants to write like that, one can also say it is "permissible," and the universe will certainly not be destroyed because of it. But I always believe that today's youths don't necessarily have to abandon vernacular writing and instead go and diligently study "Zhuangzi," learning its grammar to write articles. As for leaving it unexamined, that is certainly possible, but what harm is there in discussing it? Mr. Shi, regarding the clumsy and straightforward grammar and scant vocabulary of the youths, and my "reminiscing about the past," wasn't he unwilling to "leave it unexamined"?

(2) Mr. Shi believes that "selecting officials based on literary style" and advising youths to read "Zhuangzi and Selections of Refined Literature" have a difference between "coercion" and "contribution," and my analogy is not accurate. But I don't know, when Mr. Shi was a Chinese language teacher, whether he considered students' compositions that were rich in "Zhuangzi" grammar and "Selections of Refined Literature" vocabulary to be excellent, and after becoming an editor, also considered such works to be the top choice? If so, then if he were an "examiner," I think he would select officials based on "Zhuangzi and Selections of Refined Literature."

(3) Mr. Shi also cites Lu Xun's words, saying that he once said: (1) "Young people read Chinese books, the result is only not being able to write." This shows that he acknowledged that in order to be able to write, one should read more Chinese books; (2) "...I think that if one wants to study the old, it is better to rely on Zhang Zhidong's 'Book List with Answers' to find the way." This shows that he did not oppose young people reading ancient books. This is because Mr. Shi overlooked the time and environment. When he said the lines in (1), it was precisely when many people were clamoring for vernacular writing and that one must read ancient books, so those lines were aimed at them, saying that even if it were just as they said, it would only be not being able to write, and going to read ancient books would be even more harmful than not being able to write. As for (2), it clearly specifies young people studying old literature, which is vastly different from Mr. Shi's proposition, involving the general. If we want to study the history of ancient Chinese literature, don't we still have to read the "Book of Changes" and the "Book of Documents"?

In fact, Mr. Shi said that when he was filling out that book list, he was not as serious as I speculated, I think this statement is true. Let us try to imagine, if there really was such a young student, obediently following orders, after a period of painstaking effort, used "Zhuangzi's" grammar and "Selections of Refined Literature's" vocabulary to write an article expounding the morality of the "Analects," "Mencius," and "Yan Family Instructions," "wouldn't that be too ridiculous"?

However, my "nostalgia" is serious. I am not doing it to "gain more followers," nor because I hate Mr. Shi for not recommending "Hua Gai Collection: Supplement" and "False Freedom Book"; nor is there any other "motive," such as because I got fewer points when I was a student, or my manuscript was confiscated when I submitted it, and now I am using this to take personal revenge.

Two Brothers (9) 298

— Written by Maupassant, translated by Li Weike

When the ship docked, the sailor Papa Grelot, who was waiting there, took the two women by the hand and helped them ashore; then everyone entered the city. There were many idlers on the street, all those who went to the seawall every day at high tide to idle around, and they were also returning.

Mother Roland and Mrs. Lure walked in front, followed by the three men. When walking along Paris Road, they sometimes stopped in front of a hat shop or a jewelry store, carefully looking at a hat or a piece of jewelry; then, after expressing some opinions to each other, they walked away again.

In front of the Bourse Square, Old Roland, as usual, gazed at the trading port, which was full of ships and extended by other harbors, the huge hulls of the ships moored there in four or five rows, belly to belly. The countless masts leaning against the pier for several kilometers, all the masts attached to sails, rigging, and mastheads, made the gap in the city center look like a large dead forest. Some seagulls circled under this leafless forest, waiting for someone to throw some scraps into the water, then they flew straight down like a stone falling; and a young boy learning to be a sailor was installing a pulley at the top of a high mast, looking as if he was climbing up there to look for bird nests.

"Would you like to have a simple dinner with us and end the day together?" Mother Roland asked Mrs. Lure.

"That would be wonderful. I accept without hesitation. After spending a day together like this, it would be very lonely to run home alone," Mrs. Lure replied.

Pierre, who had heard these words and had long felt embarrassed by the young woman's coldness towards him, said softly, "Good, this widow is now inserting herself into our family." In recent days, he had been calling this woman "the widow." Although this term did not explain anything, it made Jean feel resentful when he heard the tone. To him, this term was sinister and contained insulting implications.

So the three men did not say a word until they reached the door of their residence. This residence was a narrow, three-story house located on Perman Street. Their maid Josephine was a nineteen-year-old girl, a cheap servant who came from the countryside, with a face particularly rich in the kind of surprise and crudeness that is found in country folk. She ran to open the door, let everyone in, and then closed the door, following her masters to the living room on the second floor, and then said, "A gentleman has come three times."

Old Roland, who couldn't help but roar every time he spoke to this maid, shouted:

"Who came, doesn't he have a name?"

She was never flustered by her master's roars, and she said again:

"A gentleman from the notary's (Nolaile) house."

"Which notary?"

"Well, let's just say from Mr. Carrou's house."
